If two *Yinghuo* (*Mars*) stars appear, similar in size and indistinguishable, and they remain close without deviating, one is *Mars* and the other the *Kangji* star. Their appearance foretells severe drought, which will end only when they retreat.

If two *Chen* stars (*Mercury*) appear, similar in size and indistinguishable, and they remain close without deviating, one is *Mercury* and the other the *Linze* star. Their appearance portends heavy rain. If the stars scatter and fall, it foretells heavy snow.

If two *Sui* stars (*Jupiter*) appear, similar in size and radiance, and they remain close without deviating, one is *Jupiter* and the other the *Qiangkou* star. Their appearance signals a great victory by bandits, which will manifest within half a year.

If two *Zhen* stars (*Saturn*) appear, similar in size and radiance, and they remain close without deviating, one is *Saturn* and the other the *Linyu* star. Their appearance foretells neighboring states invading borders, which will occur in the following two years. These are the inauspicious omens of the six *qi*’s interactions.

It is also said: Why does *Taibai* (*Venus*) resemble the Old Man star? In a year when Metal governs Heaven, it appears in the north during autumn. If it appears very similar to *Venus* but distant, its sighting in autumn indicates a frozen government that fails to enforce severity—signifying the nation’s longevity.

In a year when Wood governs Heaven, a *Jing* star appears in the east, as large as a half-moon and radiant, with light rays. Its appearance heralds the emergence of an enlightened ruler.

In a year when Water governs Heaven, a *Xianshi* star appears, resembling *Mercury*—pale blue-white, without radiance, and smaller than *Mercury*. If it appears distant, it signifies a worthy person living in seclusion, their name unknown.

In a year when Fire governs Heaven, a *Wenli* star appears, with four stars above and two below. The two lower stars resemble the body of the Dipper, small and red. Its appearance foretells a great plague, killing half the population. If seen, administer emetic medicine on the spring equinox to prevent illness.

In a year when Fire governs Heaven, a *Tianyu* star appears—one large and three small—often accompanied by yellow-red *qi*. Its appearance signals widespread epidemics with contagion. Administer diaphoretic medicine three times before the spring equinox to resolve it; reinforce the upper and supplement the lower to prevent illness.

When Wood governs Heaven, a *Maotou* star appears—large with long, radiant rays. This star must not scatter and fall; if it does, locusts will swarm across the land in the following three years, devouring farmlands.

In a year when Metal governs Heaven, if *Venus* approaches the *Corpse Star*—which resembles a palm star but is smaller, dim, and surrounded by a white *qi*—this is the *qi* of hidden corpses. It portends the slaughter of millions, with blood flowing for a thousand miles. If *Mars* also nears the *Corpse Star*, many will die, their bodies left exposed in the wild.

When Earth governs Heaven or resides in the Springs, a *Jiaose* star appears—resembling *Saturn* but smaller and not aligned with its celestial path. Its appearance heralds a year of abundant harvests. In a year when Earth governs Heaven, a great star appears in the south—large, yellow-white, and flickering with radiant rays. Called the *Zhanghuang Star*, it may linger for several nights, sometimes emitting sounds before scattering. As it scatters, red *qi* follows, then fades into yellow, vanishing. The next day, the sky remains windless and cloudless, yet turns yellow, and the sun appears dim. This is called the *qi* of Heavenly Stagnation, foretelling a great plague that will wipe out entire households. If seen, administer emetic and diaphoretic medicine to prevent illness. Should one contract this disease, induce vomiting and purging; warming or tonifying treatments must be avoided.

In a year when Fire governs Heaven, if the moon appears red, and this redness persists from its rising until midday without fading, it signifies severe drought. If Fire encroaches upon the moon’s horn, drought follows; if Water encroaches, heavy rains ensue. If the sun rises and remains dim from dawn to mid-morning without clouds, it portends disaster for the ruler. If the moon appears red and dim at its full phase, it foretells misfortune for the empress or concubines. If *Venus* suddenly turns red, a great wind will arise the next day. If black *qi* surges southward from the Northern Dipper, crossing the Milky Way to reach the Southern Winnowing Basket, heavy rains will follow.

When Metal governs Heaven, a great star appears in the northeast—large with radiant rays, accompanied by smaller stars below, faintly veiled in white *qi*. This is a *comet*, and its appearance foretells plunder and chaos. In a year when Wood governs Heaven, if *Jupiter* deviates from its path and drifts northward toward the Northern Dipper, lingering near the *Xuanleng* asterism and swaying east and west, it signals twelve years of national collapse, civilian suffering, and military strife.

If, in the hours before dawn (between midnight and the hour of the Ox), an image resembling the rising sun appears in the east—with red *qi* rising high and spreading across the eastern sky—then, after the *qi* disperses, two great stars emerge and remain visible until sunrise, this is called the *Jing Star*. Its appearance foretells national disaster and the ruin of agriculture. If *Venus* appears in the east at dawn during a yang year as the *Morning Star*, or in the west at dusk during a yin year as *Venus*, yet fails to follow its proper celestial path, it signals military chaos and governance in disarray.

If, at sunrise, white *qi* resembling an overturned boat appears in the east, it foretells mass slaughter, famine, and widespread illness. If, at dusk, clouds appear dim and not dark, on the verge of dispersing yet transforming into shapes like dragons, tigers, geese, or wild geese, it signifies treacherous ministers plotting rebellion. Whenever stars appear during the day, it portends disloyal subjects. If the Five Planets deviate from their paths, they foretell fortune or misfortune.

In a year when Wood governs the *qi* of the year and Wood governs Heaven, *Jupiter* should appear large and bright. If Wood’s *qi* aligns with the *Celestial Sign* but Wood is insufficient, Metal will overpower it, causing *Venus* to appear unusually large and bright. If *Venus* shares the same celestial path as *Jupiter*, yet *Jupiter* appears small while *Venus* dominates, their proximity foretells that seven years later, the people will fall ill—suffering from wind-dryness disorders. Treat with bitter and hot medicines, assisted by sour and neutral remedies.

In a year when Fire governs the *qi* of the year and Fire governs Heaven, if Fire aligns with the *Celestial Sign* but Water counteracts it, *Mars* should appear large, yet *Mercury* appears instead. If *Mercury* shares the same path as *Mars*, yet *Mars* is faint, three years later, the people will fall ill—suffering from cold-heat disorders. Treat with sweet and warm medicines, assisted by bitter and hot remedies.

In a year when Earth governs the *qi* of the year and Earth governs Heaven, if Earth aligns with the *Celestial Sign* but Wood overpowers it, *Saturn* should appear large, yet *Jupiter* appears instead. If *Jupiter* shares the same path as *Saturn*, yet *Saturn* is faint while *Jupiter* shines brightly nearby, eight years later, the people will fall ill—suffering from wind-dampness disorders. Treat with acrid and cooling medicines, assisted by sweet and warm remedies.

In a year when Metal governs the *qi* of the year and Metal governs Heaven, if Metal is insufficient and Fire overpowers it, *Venus* should appear large, yet *Mars* appears instead. If *Mars* shares the same path as *Venus*, yet *Venus* is faint while *Mars* blazes brightly nearby, six years later, the people will fall ill—suffering from vexing dryness. Treat with salty and cold medicines, assisted by acrid and cooling remedies.

In a year when Water governs the *qi* of the year and Water governs Heaven, if Water is insufficient and Earth overpowers it, *Mercury* should appear large, yet *Saturn* appears instead. If *Saturn* shares the same path as *Mercury*, yet *Mercury* is faint while *Saturn* shines brightly nearby, six years later, the people will fall ill—suffering from cold-dampness disorders. Treat with sour and neutral medicines, assisted by salty and cold remedies.

The years of illness are determined by the generative numbers of the Five Phases. For instance, when Wood is punished by Metal, the affliction lasts seven years—Wood’s number is three, Metal’s four, together making seven. The illness manifests as wind-dryness, a combination of Metal and Wood disorders. The treatment should first restrain Metal’s excess, then replenish Wood’s deficiency.

When Fire is punished by Water, the affliction lasts three years—Water’s number is one, Fire’s two, together making three. The illness manifests as cold-heat, a combination of Water and Fire disorders. The treatment should first restrain Water’s dominance, then replenish Fire’s deficiency.

When Earth is punished by Wood, the affliction lasts eight years—Wood’s number is three, Earth’s five, together making eight. The illness manifests as wind-dampness, a combination of Wood and Earth disorders. The treatment should first restrain Wood’s dominance, then replenish Earth’s deficiency.

When Metal is punished by Fire, the affliction lasts six years—Fire’s number is two, Metal’s four, together making six. The illness manifests as vexing dryness, a combination of Fire and Metal disorders. The treatment should first restrain Fire’s dominance, then replenish Metal’s deficiency.

When Water is punished by Earth, the affliction lasts six years—Water’s number is one, Earth’s five, together making six. The illness manifests as cold-dampness, a combination of Water and Earth disorders. The treatment should first restrain Earth’s excess, then replenish Water’s deficiency.

In all years of mutual conquest and retaliation, if the stars do not share the same celestial degree or do not overcome one another, these symptoms will not appear. If there is only mutual conquest and retaliation without subjugation between the stars, there will be no such illness or disaster.

The sun’s radiant majesty is the great standard of luminous order, the guiding principle of light and shadow, the essence of all yang, and the symbol of all nobility. When the sun is vast and its light travels unimpeded, the world knows peace. When the sun rises with a white glow, yang lacks virtue. When the sun sets without light, yang suffers punishment. When the sun’s light shines brilliantly, the ruler falls ill. When the sun has risen a pole’s height yet remains dim and colorless without clouds, the people suffer. When the sun is two poles from setting in the west yet remains dim, people die. When the sun passes midday yet remains half-dark, the ruler’s Way is deficient, and the people lose their livelihood.

When the sun has two "feet," many warlords rise. When the sun shows red "feet," the state faces urgent invasion. When the sun hangs with "fangs," barbarians invade, and generals are deployed. When the sun has "double ears," the Son of Heaven gains territory. When a yellow aura embraces the sun, the chief minister is inwardly loyal. When the sun darkens at midday, failing to emerge, great floods occur. When the sun is dark at noon, yin prevails, and treacherous ministers control the ruler.

When the sun has black light, within sixty days the five grains will be damaged, and great floods will come. When the sun has six "ears," within sixty days the state will perish. When the sun has a red aura like a crown at its side, or "ears" appear with a grasping form, and the shape suggests warfare, great winds will rise, followed by violent rain. When the spring sun has four "ears," the Son of Heaven will have a grandson within three years.

When an aura like a tiger strikes the sun, a general will rebel. When a green dragon guards the sun, ministers plot against the ruler. When green qi rises above and below the sun, it is auspicious to deploy troops. When green and red qi obscure the rising sun, a great battle is certain. When the sun has a tiger-like red aura at its side, ten thousand will die. When the sun is colorless, or a red qi like a star leaps within it, the ruler faces misfortune.

When an aura two feet wide appears east or west of the sun, the state will face sorrow and war. When a black qi like a coiled dragon appears above the sun, great winds will come. At the winter solstice, if clouds greet and send off the sun at sunrise and sunset, the year will bring epidemics among the people. Red clouds foretell drought, white clouds war, yellow clouds plague, black clouds great floods, and green clouds great winds.

When the sun has a double yellow halo, winds and rains will come in season, bringing abundant harvests and low prices. When the sun has a white halo, within ninety days violent warfare will erupt, the year will see many sudden illnesses, and nobles will fall sick. When the sun has a triple green halo, the state will face excessive wind and rain; within ninety days, the queen will suffer disaster, and winter thunder or summer snow will occur.

When the sun has a double red halo, the disaster will strike below; the land where it appears will suffer locusts, two hundred days of drought, high grain prices, rampant banditry, and minor military conflicts. When the sun has four halos, the Four Seas will see war, lasting one year. When the sun’s halo is half-formed like a cauldron lid, it portends reconciliation with a distant and harmonious state. When the sun has three halos, the feudal lords will rebel. When the sun has five halos, the year will bring famine and high grain prices. When the sun has ten halos, the world will perish, the earth will yield nothing, and this will last five years.

When a star falls as earth, great famine and bloodshed follow. When a star falls as sand, armies are defeated and states perish. When a star falls as metal, great war arises. When a star falls as stone, disaster strikes those below. When a white rainbow appears, or Saturn scatters into a rainbow, and a white rainbow emerges beneath it, blood will flow. When a white rainbow pierces the sun, close ministers will betray the ruler. When a white rainbow appears in the east in summer, wheat will be expensive. Wherever a white rainbow appears, the state will see killing. When a white rainbow circles a city but does not complete the loop, the side from which it comes will prevail in attack.

When a rainbow appears in the west, the year will bring disaster to women. When a rainbow arches over a city, blood will flow beneath it. When a red rainbow descends straight from the heavens to point at a state, that land will face chaos and ruin. When a rainbow bends like a snake with its head pointing downward, the people below will fall ill. When a rainbow appears with the sun in the east, the year will be inauspicious. When a rainbow lingers to the left of the sun without dissipating, those who see it will face disaster.

When a white qi appears below Venus, great war will come. When a green qi appears below Jupiter, great winds will come. When a yellow qi appears below Saturn, great plague will come. When a black qi appears below Mercury, great floods will come. When a red qi appears below Mars, great drought will come. When the moon has a halo with a star inside, great winds will come. When a black qi appears behind the moon, great rains will come.

When the moon has a shadow like a small moon above it, the state will face conflict. When the moon has a double halo, wind and rain will come. When the moon has four halos, the four gates of the state will face chaos and misgovernance. When the moon’s halo has clouds like hands at its side, the people will face disaster. When the moon has three large "feet" below it, ten thousand will die. When the moon should be full but is not, and white clouds follow it on all sides, the queen will face disaster. When the moon’s two horns have large stars, the people will face disaster.

When a large star appears behind the moon, with many small stars below, hail will come. When a black qi emerges from the moon and turns red, on the third day a black wind will come. When a white qi emerges from the moon, great snow will come. When Venus moves through the constellations with its rays sharp above and broad below, advancing and retreating in proper measure, appearing at the appointed time, the world will prosper. When Venus is high, small, and bright, shining without rays, it portends great peace. When Venus is large and radiant with rays, it portends warfare.

When Venus enters the moon and the star’s color is distinct, ministers plot against the ruler. When the moon eclipses Venus like a solar eclipse, loyal ministers will be executed. When Venus appears in the west, the moon in the north, and a star in the north, the state will face powerful warfare.

When a star appears south of the moon, Chinese armies will prevail in the southern lands. When Venus and the moon draw near, if the space between them allows three fingers’ breadth, it portends warfare; if two fingers’ breadth, it portends city distress.

When Venus lies north of Saturn, lands will be lost and the state will perish. When Venus stands high and bright in the west, appearing early, it portends a powerful army. When Venus appears in the east and remains visible after sunrise, it portends armed conflict.

When Venus should appear but does not, it is inauspicious. When many stars gather beside the moon, encircling it once like a courtyard wall, it portends the state’s victory. When a purple qi swirls around the moon, the empress and consorts possess virtue.

When the moon is full and bright, its brightness vast and still as if motionless, the empress and consorts possess virtue. When the moon is full yet dim, lacking radiance, the empress and consorts face calamity. When the moon remains bright even in daylight, the ruler lacks virtue.

*Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu, Scroll Three concludes*

*Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu, Scroll Four*
*Recorded by Qi Xuzi*

**Heavenly Cycles and Their Annual Encounters**

**Jiazi Year (1st Celestial Stem, 1st Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zheng* phase prevails. Lesser Yin’s sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The earthly *qi* of the year aligns harmoniously with fire, for fire engenders earth. The heat transformation is seven—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Below, it encroaches upon the lung *qi*; above, white *qi* ascends to serve heaven, signifying the dominance of the long *qi*. Great summer heat spreads, and the people suffer from panting, coughing, alternating chills and fever, snoring, sneezing, and nasal congestion—all rooted in the lung. The *jia*-type insects perish. When the triumph is extreme, water arrives to retaliate, and the cold *qi* reverses its function. The heart viscera fall ill, feathered insects emerge, and the summer heat of heaven turns to cold. The celestial body *Chenxing* (Mercury) appears abnormally large, while *Genhuang* (a stellar marker) dims.

**Jiawu Year (7th Celestial Stem, 7th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zheng* phase prevails. Lesser Yin’s sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The heat transformation is two—a number derived from the stem’s generation. The long *qi* flourishes, great summer heat spreads, the lung *qi* rises, and white *qi* serves heaven. The lung falls ill, and *jia*-type insects perish. The people suffer from heat prevailing above. Treat with salty-cold substances, for water’s nature and flavor subdue the triumph of fire-heat. Avoid consuming bitter-heat foods, which would aid fire’s dominance. Above, *Genhuang* shines brightly, while *Taibai* (Venus) loses its luster.

**Yichou Year (2nd Celestial Stem, 2nd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. Greater Yin’s earth governs heaven. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The year’s metal *qi* and heaven’s earth mutually engender, and the rain transformation is five. Below, it suppresses the kidney *qi*, which weakens; black *qi* serves heaven, and the transforming *qi* triumphs. Damp *qi* flourishes, the kidney viscera fall ill, and the illness lingers in the bladder. Scaled insects perish. The people suffer from impotence, extreme debility with intermittent recovery, lumbar pain, and difficulty in movement. When the triumph is extreme, wood arrives to retaliate. Great winds arise frequently, and the people suffer from spleen and stomach ailments. *Baochong*-type insects perish. *Suixing* (Jupiter) appears abnormally, while *Zhenxing* (Saturn) dims.

**Yiwei Year (2nd Celestial Stem, 8th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. Greater Yin’s earth governs heaven, with dampness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The rain transformation is five. Below, it encroaches upon the kidney viscera, which fall ill, and the illness lingers in the bladder. Scaled insects perish. The triumph of rain and dampness causes the people to suffer from flaccid paralysis, cold limbs, chills in the channels, impotence, and weakness. Treat with salty-neutral substances, using wood’s flavor and nature to balance the triumph of earth’s dampness. *Zhenxing* appears large, while *Chenxing* loses its luster.

**Bingyin Year (3rd Celestial Stem, 3rd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zheng* phase prevails. Lesser Yang’s ministerial fire governs heaven. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The heat transformation is two—a number derived from the stem’s generation. The long *qi* flourishes. Below, it encroaches upon the lung viscera, which fall ill, and the illness lingers in the large intestine. *Jia*-type insects perish. The people suffer from heat diseases prevailing above, all marked by vexation, fullness, and oppressive heat. Treat with salty-cold substances, for water’s flavor and nature subdue the flourishing of fire-heat. Avoid consuming bitter-heat foods, which would aid fire’s triumph. *Yinghuo* (Mars) appears large, while *Taibai* diminishes.

**Bingshen Year (3rd Celestial Stem, 9th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zheng* phase prevails. Lesser Yang’s ministerial fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The heat transformation is seven—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Below, it encroaches upon the lung *qi*; above, white *qi* serves heaven. Summer heat governs autumn’s administration, but the contracting *qi* fails to command. The lung viscera fall ill, and *jia*-type insects perish. The people suffer from heat above, coughing, and panting. When the triumph is profound, water arrives to retaliate. The cold mandate arrives early, feathered insects suffer, and the people fall ill with alternating chills and fever in the heart. The lung receives the water *qi*, and metal in *shen* (9th Earthly Branch) assists it, reducing the illness by half. *Chenxing* appears abnormally, while *Yinghuo* dims.

**Dingmao Year (4th Celestial Stem, 4th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. Yang Brightness’ metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. Below, it encroaches upon the liver viscera, and furred insects perish—yet none of these manifestations appear. Why? *Ding* is a wood year, and the year’s *qi* is assisted by *mao* wood. In the first month, *renyin*, *ding* combines with *ren*, gaining the strength of the celestial stems. Moreover, this is called a "yearly convergence," thus achieving balanced *qi*. Yang Brightness above cannot harm it. The dry transformation is nine—a number derived from the branch’s completion. *Taibai* shines brightly.

**Dingyou Year (4th Celestial Stem, 10th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. Yang Brightness’ metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The dry transformation is four—a number derived from the stem’s generation. *You* is metal, and this is called a "heavenly tally." Below, it encroaches upon the liver *qi*; above, green *qi* rises to serve heaven. Chill and desolation arrive frequently, trees are felled, and grasses wither. The people suffer from hypochondriac pain, red eyes, tremors, shivering, and muscle atrophy, rendering them unable to stand for long. Treat with bitter-heat substances, for fire’s flavor and nature can subdue metal’s ailments. Avoid consuming acrid-cold foods, which would aid metal’s triumph. *Taibai* shines brightly, while *Suixing* diminishes.

**Wuchen Year (5th Celestial Stem, 5th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. Greater Yang’s cold water governs heaven, with cold prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The cold transformation is six—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Below, it encroaches upon the heart viscera; red *qi* ascends, water freezes, and fire *qi* rises high. The people suffer from heart ailments, and feathered insects perish. When the triumph is extreme, earth’s rain arrives to retaliate. The kidney *qi* falls ill in turn, and scaled insects also perish. *Chenxing* dims, while *Zhenxing* brightens. Earth’s retaliation prevails, and the heart viscera’s illness is halved.

**Wuxu Year (5th Celestial Stem, 11th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. Greater Yang’s cold water governs heaven. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The cold transformation is one—a number derived from the stem’s generation. Treat with sweet-warm substances, for these are earth’s nature and flavor. Avoid consuming salty-cold foods, which would aid water’s triumph. Above, *Chenxing* shines brightly, while *Yinghuo* loses its luster. Its mandate follows the previous pattern, except without retaliation.

**Jisi Year (6th Celestial Stem, 6th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. Reverting Yin governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The wind transformation is eight—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Below, it encroaches upon the spleen *qi*; above, earth’s *qi* rises and flourishes. *Baochong*-type insects perish, yellow *qi* emerges, water turns green, and earth’s function is transformed.

The body grows heavy, muscles wither, appetite declines, and taste dulls. Wind lifts the great void, clouds and objects sway and tremble, eyes spin and ears ring. When the triumph is extreme, metal retaliates: dryness arrives, white dust rises, the spleen is preserved, *baochong*-type insects remain still, *Taibai* reappears, and *Suixing* diminishes again.

**Jihai Year (6th Celestial Stem, 12th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. Reverting Yin governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The wind transformation is three—a number derived from the stem’s generative count. The people suffer from wind-borne illnesses above. Treat with pungent-cold substances, for these are metal’s nature and flavor. Avoid consuming sour-harmonizing foods, which would aid wood’s triumph. Above, *Suixing* shines brightly and greatly, while *Zhenxing* dims and recedes.

**Gengwu Year (7th Celestial Stem, 7th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. Lesser Yin sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The heat transformation is two—a number derived from the stem’s generative count. Wu is the southern fire, and here Lesser Yin sovereign fire appears, termed "Heavenly Conformity." Below, it encroaches upon the lung *qi*; above, white *qi* ascends. *Jiachong*-type insects perish, metal’s function turns to grass and wood, with wheezing, vomiting, alternating chills and fever, sneezing, hiccups, and nasal congestion. Great heat spreads, heaven triumphs over the phase, the phase is excessive, and the lungs are aided. *Jiachong* receive *qi*, and metal’s calamity is half-mitigated. *Haohuang* shines brightly, and *Taibai* does likewise.

**Gengzi Year (7th Celestial Stem, 1st Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. Lesser Yin sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The heat transformation is seven—a number derived from the branch’s completion. The people suffer from heat-borne illnesses above. Great heat spreads, the long *qi* triumphs, and when the triumph is extreme, water retaliates: sudden cold arrives, the heart is afflicted, *yuchong*-type insects perish, *Chenxing* shines brightly again, and *Haohuang* diminishes.

**Xinwei Year (8th Celestial Stem, 8th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. Greater Yin earth governs heaven, with dampness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The rain transformation is five. Below, it encroaches upon the kidney *qi*; above, black *qi* ascends. Scaled insects perish, water turns turbid, and misty rain sinks into darkness. The chest is discomforted, Yin wilts, *qi* greatly declines and fails to rise or move. At this time, the lower back and spine ache, movement is difficult, and the people suffer from swelling. Dampness prevails above. Treat with sour-harmonizing substances, for these are wood’s nature and flavor. Avoid consuming sweet-warm foods, which would aid earth’s triumph. Above, *Zhenxing* appears greatly, while *Chenxing* dims.

**Xinchou Year (8th Celestial Stem, 2nd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. Greater Yin earth governs heaven, with dampness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The rain transformation is five. Below, it encroaches upon the kidney viscera, which falls ill, eventually affecting the bladder. Scaled insects are distressed, transformative *qi* is abundant, and visceral *qi* loses its command. When the triumph is extreme, wood retaliates: great winds arise, the spleen is afflicted, *baochong*-type insects suffer calamity, *Zhenxing* recedes, and *Suixing* reappears.

**Renshen Year (9th Celestial Stem, 9th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. Lesser Yang ministerial fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The heat transformation is seven—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Below, it encroaches upon the lung *qi*; above, white *qi* ascends. Metal’s function turns to grass and wood, fire appears scorching, metal is transformed and depleted. Great heat spreads, metal is distressed, and water retaliates: sudden cold arrives in summer, the heart is afflicted, *yuchong*-type insects perish, *Yinghuo* appears greatly and brightly, while *Taibai* diminishes.

**Renyin Year (9th Celestial Stem, 3rd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. Lesser Yang ministerial fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The heat transformation is two—a number derived from the stem’s generative count. Below, it encroaches upon the lung viscera, which falls ill, eventually affecting the large intestine. *Jiachong*-type insects perish. The people suffer from heat-borne illnesses above. Treat with salty-cold substances, for these are water’s nature and flavor. Avoid consuming bitter-hot foods, which would aid fire’s triumph. *Yinghuo* shines brightly, while *Taibai* diminishes.

**Guiyou Year (10th Celestial Stem, 10th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. Yang Brilliance metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The dryness transformation is four—a number derived from the stem’s generative count. You is the western metal, and here Yang Brilliance metal appears above, termed "Heavenly Conformity." The people suffer from dryness prevailing above. Treat with bitter-hot substances, for these are fire’s nature and flavor. Avoid consuming pungent-cold foods, which would aid metal’s triumph. Above, *Taibai* shines brilliantly, and *Suixing* brightens again.

**Guimao Year (10th Celestial Stem, 4th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. Yang Brilliance metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The dryness transformation is nine—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Below, it encroaches upon the liver *qi*; above, green *qi* ascends. Fur-bearing insects perish, wood’s function is established, earth turns green, and cold winds arrive repeatedly. Grass withers under wood’s assault. Rib pain, eye twitching, trembling, and shivering occur, sinews weaken, and one cannot stand for long. When the triumph is extreme, fire retaliates: scorching heat arrives in summer, the lungs are afflicted, *jiachong*-type insects suffer calamity again, *Yinghuo* appears, and *Taibai* dims.

**Jiaxu Year (1st Celestial Stem, 11th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. Greater Yang cold water governs heaven, with cold prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The cold transformation is one—a number derived from the stem’s generative count. Below, it encroaches upon the heart viscera; red *qi* ascends, fire brightens and turns vermilion, *yuchong*-type insects thrive, long *qi* turns cold, gathering *qi* is balanced, and visceral *qi* is excessive. The people suffer from cold prevailing above. Treat with sweet-warm substances, for these are earth’s nature and flavor. Avoid consuming salty-cold foods, which would aid water’s triumph. Above, *Chenxing* appears greatly, while *Yinghuo* dims.

**Jiachen Year (1st Celestial Stem, 5th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. Greater Yang cold water governs heaven, with cold prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The cold transformation is six—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Below, it encroaches upon the heart viscera; red *qi* ascends, *yuchong*-type insects suffer calamity, metal announces distress, and cold mists rise at dawn. When the triumph is extreme, water freezes, and fire’s *qi* shines brightly above.

The heart grows hot, vexed, and full; the throat dries, and thirst arises frequently. Sighing, sneezing, sorrow, and frequent yawning follow. As heat *qi* ascends, cold retaliates—frost descends untimely, forgetfulness and heart pain arise. When the triumph is extreme, earth retaliates: rain and dampness settle into deep yin, the kidney suffers illness, and scaled creatures likewise. *Zhenxing* dims, while *Chenxing* hides in concealment.

**Yihai Year (2nd Celestial Stem, 12th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. Greater Yin governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The wind transformation is three—a number derived from the root’s generative count. Generative *qi* flourishes, transformative *qi* loses command, and visceral *qi* naturally balances. The spleen viscera falls ill, and fur-bearing creatures suffer harm. The people’s afflictions arise from wind prevailing above; treat with acrid-cold substances, for these are metal’s nature and flavor. Avoid consuming sour-harmonizing foods, which would aid wood’s triumph. *Suixing* shines brightly, while *Zhenxing* dims and shrinks.

**Yisi Year (2nd Celestial Stem, 6th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. Greater Yin governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The wind transformation is eight—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Generative *qi* transforms, exuberant *qi* loses command, and visceral *qi* naturally balances. Fur-bearing creatures suffer calamity; the spleen is harmed, causing abdominal fullness, distension, belching, and hiccups. When the triumph is extreme, metal retaliates—this is called "retaliatory triumph." Cold vigor arrives, grasses and trees wither, and frost and dew descend. The people suffer abdominal distension; treat with bitter-heat to punish metal’s triumph, aiding with acrid-cold. Due to metal’s insufficiency, *Taibai* dims, while *Suixing* shrinks.

**Bingzi Year (3rd Celestial Stem, 1st Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. Lesser Yin sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The heat transformation is seven—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Heat *qi* descends below, lung *qi* ascends in compliance, white *qi* serves heaven, metal is employed, shell creatures suffer calamity, and grasses and trees announce distress. Wheezing, vomiting, alternating chills and fever, sneezing, nasal congestion, and obstruction follow. Great heat spreads—why does metal’s calamity reach only half? The year’s water *qi* is excessive, triumphing over heaven; heavenly command is half-diminished, and water does not retaliate. Above, *Yinghuo* shines brightly.

**Bingwu Year (3rd Celestial Stem, 7th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. Lesser Yin sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The heat transformation is two—a number derived from the root’s generative count. Wu is southern fire; Lesser Yin sovereign fire is called "heavenly tally in accord." Though the year’s *qi* is water, one water cannot overcome two fires—thus it differs from *Bingzi*. Greater *qi* flourishes, gathering *qi* wanes, and visceral *qi* is balanced. The lung viscera falls ill, and shell creatures suffer calamity. The people’s afflictions arise from heat prevailing above; treat with salty-cold, for these are water’s nature and flavor, capable of subduing fiery-heat illnesses. Avoid consuming bitter-heat foods, which would aid fire’s triumph. *Yinghuo* is great, while *Taibai* is small.

**Dingchou Year (4th Celestial Stem, 2nd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. Greater Yin rain-earth governs heaven, with dampness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The damp transformation is five. Damp *qi* descends below, the kidney viscera falls ill, and black *qi* ascends in compliance with heaven. Water transforms into dust, obscuring clouds and rain. The chest feels unwell, yang wilts, *qi* greatly declines and fails to rise or function. When retaliation occurs, lumbar and flank pain arise. If dampness triumphs long, wind-wood retaliates, transformative command falters, and fur-bearing creatures suffer calamity—the spleen and abdomen fall ill. *Zhenxing* dims, while *Suixing* shines again.

**Dingwei Year (4th Celestial Stem, 8th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. Greater Yin rain-earth governs heaven, with dampness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The damp transformation is five. Wood’s *qi* is balanced, and heavenly command is half-diminished. Though transformative *qi* triumphs, generative *qi* naturally balances, visceral *qi* is slight, scaled creatures avoid calamity, and kidney illness is minor. The people suffer swelling, with dampness prevailing above; treat with sour, aiding with balanced flavors. Avoid consuming sweet-warm foods. *Zhenxing* shines brightly.

**Wuyin Year (5th Celestial Stem, 3rd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. Lesser Yang ministerial fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. The summerheat transformation is two—a number derived from the root’s generative count. Fire-heat transforms greatly in the center. The year’s *Wufire* *qi* is excessive, aligning in virtue with the heavenly tally above and descending upon the lung *qi* below. Shell creatures perish, and those with chronic lung illness die. The people suffer upper heat with vexation and fullness; prolonged illness reaches the large intestine, causing bloody stool and hemorrhage. Greater *qi* blazes in command, gathering *qi* loses governance, and generative *qi* naturally balances. Treat with salty-cold, employing water’s nature and flavor to extinguish fire’s exuberance. Avoid consuming bitter-heat foods, which would aid fire’s dominance. *Yinghuo* shines brightly, while *Taibai* loses its luster.

**Wushen Year (5th Celestial Stem, 9th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. Lesser Yang ministerial fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. The heat transformation is seven—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Fire *qi* descends upon lung *qi*, white *qi* ascends in compliance with heaven. Metal is employed, grasses and trees wither, fire appears scorching, and metal is reformed yet depleted. Great heat arises, and the people suffer wheezing and coughing. Shell creatures perish prematurely. Though the triumph is extreme, metal gains the year’s strength—*Shenmetal* aids it, and water retaliates. Heat prevails yet ultimately cools; the heart falls ill, feathered creatures suffer calamity again, and *Yinghuo* shrinks.

**Jimao Year (6th Celestial Stem, 4th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. Yangming metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet inviting retaliation. Though metal and the year’s earth *qi* harmonize, the *Zi-Wu* fire positions are adverse. The dryness transformation is nine—a number derived from the branch’s completion. Below, it encroaches upon liver *qi*; above, blue-green *qi* ascends in compliance with heaven. Wood is employed, fur-bearing creatures suffer calamity, earth announces distress, and cold vigor arrives repeatedly. Wood is felled, grasses wither. The people suffer rib-side pain, red eyes, and sinew wilting. Though the triumph is extreme, wood gains the year’s strength—*Maowood* aids it, preventing decline. Fire retaliates next, dryness yields to summerheat, the lung is again distressed, shell creatures suffer calamity, *Taibai* dims, and *Yinghuo* shines again.

**Jiyou Year (6th Celestial Stem, 10th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. Yangming metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation.

**You Year (10th Earthly Branch, Metal):**
This is named "Heavenly Conformity." Two metals combine, and the earthly *qi* of the phase harmonizes. Dryness transforms by four, following its generative number. Generative *qi* is lost, wood withers, the liver organ suffers illness, and in time the gallbladder is affected. Fur-bearing creatures are distressed, the *qi* of harvest prevails, and the killing force arrives early. Wood turns blue-green and falls; the people suffer from dryness diseases above. Treat with bitter heat—the nature and flavor of fire. *Taibai* shines brightly, while *Suixing* loses its luster.

**Gengchen Year (7th Celestial Stem, 5th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. *Taiyang* cold water governs heaven, with cold prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Cold transforms by six, following its standard completion number. Below, it approaches heart *qi*; above, fire *qi* ascends in compliance. Metal turns blue-green, and when cold and desolation arise, water freezes. Fire *qi* rises high and bright, and illness returns to the heart, in time affecting the small intestine. Feathered creatures perish. When the triumph is extreme, earth sends rain in retaliation, bringing dust and dampness. Clouds and rain arrive, the kidneys generate illness, and scaled creatures suffer. *Chenxing* disappears, while *Zhenxing* regains its brightness.

**Gengxu Year (7th Celestial Stem, 11th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. *Taiyang* cold water governs heaven, with cold prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Cold transforms by one, following its generative number. The *qi* of storage is biting, the *qi* of growth is cold and restrained, and the *qi* of harvest is properly aligned. The people suffer from cold diseases above. Treat with sweet warmth—the nature and flavor of earth. Do not use salty cold, lest it aid water’s triumph.

*Chenxing* appears large, while *Yinghuo* dims.

**Xinsi Year (8th Celestial Stem, 6th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. *Jueyin* wood governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Wind transforms by eight, following its standard completion number. Below, it approaches spleen *qi*; above, earth *qi* ascends and flourishes. Yellow *qi* arises, water turns blue-green, and earth’s function is altered. The body feels heavy, muscles wither, appetite diminishes, and the mouth loses its sense of taste. Wind spreads across the great void, and clouds and objects sway. The eyes spin and the ears ring. When the triumph runs deep, metal issues its decree, white dust rises on all sides, and the liver suffers illness again. Fur-bearing creatures are harmed in turn. *Suixing* dims again, while *Taibai* regains its brilliance.

**Xinhai Year (8th Celestial Stem, 12th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. *Jueyin* wood governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Wind transforms by three, following its generative number. Generative *qi* asserts its command, grasses and trees flourish, transformative *qi* is deficient, and rain and dampness fail to prevail. The *qi* of storage is properly aligned. The people suffer from spleen diseases, and shelled creatures are distressed. Wind diseases prevail above. Treat with acrid cold—the nature and flavor of metal. Do not eat sour foods, lest they aid wood’s dominion.

*Suixing* shines with radiance, while *Zhenxing* dims.

**Renwu Year (9th Celestial Stem, 7th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. *Shaoyin* sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Heat transforms by two, following its generative number. The *qi* of growth blazes, the *qi* of harvest loses its command, and generative *qi* is properly aligned. The lung organ generates illness, and in time the large intestine is affected. Scaled creatures suffer calamity. The people suffer from heat diseases above. Treat with salty cold—water’s flavor and nature—to suppress fire’s heat. Do not eat bitter hot foods, lest they aid the heart’s dominion.

*Yinghuo* blazes brightly, while *Taibai* loses its luster.

**Renzi Year (9th Celestial Stem, 1st Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. *Shaoyin* sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Heat’s command approaches lung *qi* below; above, white *qi* ascends in compliance. Metal is employed, grasses and trees turn blue-green, and scaled creatures suffer calamity. When the triumph runs deep, water retaliates. When retaliation arrives, early summer brings cold, and illness returns severely to the heart. Feathered creatures are distressed. *Chenxing* shines again, while *Yinghuo* disappears.

**Guiwei Year (10th Celestial Stem, 8th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. *Taiyin* earth governs heaven, with dampness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Rain transforms by five; rain triumphs over transformative *qi*, and the command is properly aligned. The *qi* of storage is not biting, and the *qi* of growth asserts its command. The kidney organ suffers illness, and scaled creatures suffer calamity. The people suffer from swelling and dampness above. Treat with sourness, harmonizing with wood’s nature and flavor to balance earth’s triumph.

*Zhenxing* shines with radiance, while *Chenyao* disappears.

**Guichou Year (10th Celestial Stem, 2nd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. *Taiyin* earth governs heaven, with dampness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Rain transforms by five. Below, it approaches kidney *qi*; above, black *qi* arises. Water turns to ice, dust veils clouds and rain, and the chest is discomforted. Scaled creatures perish, and those with depleted kidney *qi* die. When the triumph endures, wood sends wind in retaliation. Great winds arise at times, shelled creatures are distressed, and the spleen suffers illness in turn.

*Suixing* shines brightly, while *Zhenxing* brightens then diminishes.

**Jiashen Year (1st Celestial Stem, 9th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. *Shaoyang* ministerial fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Heat transforms by seven, following its standard completion number. Below, it approaches lung *qi*; above, white *qi* ascends in compliance with heaven. Scaled creatures suffer calamity, metal is employed, and grasses announce distress. Fire appears in brilliance, altering and depleting metal. Great summerheat asserts its command, and water retaliates with cold. When cold arrives, the heart suffers illness, and feathered creatures suffer calamity.

*Chenxing* appears large, while *Yinghuo* diminishes.

**Jiayin Year (1st Celestial Stem, 3rd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. *Shaoyang* ministerial fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Heat transforms by two, following its generative number. The *qi* of growth blazes, the *qi* of harvest is unclear, and generative *qi* asserts its command. Scaled creatures perish, the lung organ suffers illness, and in time the large intestine is affected. The people suffer from heat diseases above. Treat with salty cold—water’s flavor and nature—to suppress fire’s heat. Do not eat bitter hot foods, lest they aid fire’s dominion.

*Yinghuo* shines brightly, while *Taibai* loses its luster.

**Yiyou Year (2nd Celestial Stem, 10th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. *Yangming* metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Dryness transforms by four, following its generative number. Generative *qi* fails to transform, the *qi* of harvest is excessive, and transformative *qi* is properly aligned. Below, it approaches the liver organ, which suffers illness, and in time the gallbladder is affected. Fur-bearing creatures perish.

The people suffer from dryness prevailing above. Treat with bitter heat—fire’s nature and fire’s flavor. Do not eat pungent frozen foods, lest they aid metal’s dominion.

The *qi* of the center aligns with metal’s movement, and the movement harmonizes with heaven’s virtue, called the *Taiyi Heavenly Conformity*, a triple convergence. *You* is metal, the movement is metal, and the *qi* governing heaven is metal. *Taibai* shines brightly, while *Suixing* appears small.

**Yimao Year (2nd Celestial Stem, 4th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. *Yangming* metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its oppositional transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Dryness transforms by nine, following its resultant number. Below, it approaches the liver’s *qi*; above, the verdant *qi* ascends to serve heaven. Wood is employed and established, earth turns green, and the generative cycle arrives—wood fells grasses, causing them to wither. The people suffer from rib pain, red eyes, tremors, shivering, and muscle spasms; their sinews atrophy, preventing prolonged standing. Fur-bearing creatures perish in disaster. When triumph is profound, fire retaliates. Heat transforms in autumn’s proper alignment, and the killing force does not arrive; dryness’s command is untimely, and the lung falls ill. Scaled creatures suffer disaster in reverse, *Yinghuo* appears large, and *Taibai* diminishes again.

**Bingxu Year (3rd Celestial Stem, 11th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. *Taiyang* cold water governs heaven, with cold prevailing above. Its upright transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Cold transforms by one, following its generative number. The *Bing* water movement is excessive, harmonizing with heaven’s virtue, called a *Heavenly Conformity*. The *qi* of the organs transforms with severity; the *qi* of growth loses its command, and the *qi* of harvest aligns properly. Below, it approaches the heart organ, which suffers illness, and in time the small intestine is affected. Feathered creatures perish. The people suffer from cold diseases above. Treat with sweet warmth—earth’s nature and earth’s flavor. Do not eat salty cold foods, lest they aid water’s dominion. *Chenxing* appears large, while *Yinghuo* loses its luster.

**Bingchen Year (3rd Celestial Stem, 5th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. *Taiyang* cold water governs heaven, with cold prevailing above. Its oppositional transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Cold transforms by six, following its resultant number. Below, it approaches the heart organ; above, it follows the fiery red *qi* ascending to serve heaven. Metal turns green, and water’s cold naturally triumphs over the *qi* of growth. Feathered creatures perish, and those with chronic heart illness die. When triumph is profound, earth’s rains arrive, and earth’s transformation is hindered. Dust and dampness revive, and continuous rain falls. Kidney illness arises, and scaled creatures suffer disaster in reverse. *Zhenxing* shines brightly, while *Chenyao* conceals itself—this is called a *Heavenly Conformity*, and the retaliation is half-suppressed.

**Dinghai Year (4th Celestial Stem, 12th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. *Jueyin* wood governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its upright transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Wind transforms by three, following its generative number. The *qi* of transformation loses its command, while the *qi* of storage aligns properly. The spleen organ suffers illness, and scaled creatures perish in disaster. The people suffer from wind diseases prevailing above. Treat with pungent cold—metal’s flavor and metal’s nature—to suppress wood’s triumph. Do not eat sour foods, lest they aid wood’s dominion. The movement harmonizes with heaven, called a *Heavenly Conformity* year. *Suixing* appears large and bright, while *Zhenxing* is dim and small.

**Dingsi Year (4th Celestial Stem, 6th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. *Jueyin* wood governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its oppositional transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Wind transforms by eight, following its resultant number. Below, it approaches the spleen’s *qi*; above, it follows the dust-laden *qi* ascending to serve heaven. Water turns green, muscles atrophy, appetite diminishes, and flavors fade. Wind stirs the great void, and clouds and objects sway. The people suffer from dizziness and tinnitus. Scaled creatures languish. When triumph is profound, dry metal arrives, and white dust obscures the great void. Leaves wither and fall before yellowing, and the liver suffers illness in reverse. Fur-bearing creatures perish in disaster. *Suixing* diminishes again, while *Taibai* regains brightness. This is not a *Heavenly Conformity*, and its disasters are severe.

**Wuzi Year (5th Celestial Stem, 1st Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. *Shaoyin* sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its oppositional transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Heat transforms by seven, following its resultant number. The *Wu* fire movement achieves *Heavenly Conformity*. Below, it approaches the lung’s *qi*; above, it follows the white *qi* ascending to serve heaven. Wood turns green, fire appears blazing, and metal is greatly depleted. The lung falls ill, and scaled creatures perish in disaster. Before long, water retaliates, bringing sudden cold. Summer’s command wanes, and its time is diminished. Heart illness arises, and feathered creatures perish. *Chenxing* appears at dawn, while *Yinghuo* sinks small in the evening. Later, it surpasses the *Heavenly Conformity*, and the triumph is minor.

**Wuwu Year (5th Celestial Stem, 7th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zhi* phase prevails. *Shaoyin* sovereign fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. The *Wu* fire movement, the *Wu* year, and *Shaoyin* fire converge—called the *Taiyi Heavenly Conformity*, a triple convergence. Its upright transformation is abundant and substantial, with triumph even more severe, yet no retaliation occurs. Heat transforms by two, following its generative number. The *qi* of growth scorches, the *qi* of harvest remains hot, and the *qi* of generation aligns properly. Feathered creatures transform, while scaled creatures perish in disaster. Those with chronic lung illness die. The people suffer from heat diseases above, with unceasing vexation and thirst. Treat with salty cold—water’s flavor and water’s nature—to suppress fire’s heat. Do not eat bitter hot foods, lest they aid the heart’s dominion. *Yinghuo* and *Genhuang* appear twice, while *Taibai* conceals itself.

**Jichou Year (6th Celestial Stem, 2nd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. *Taiyin* earth governs heaven, with dampness prevailing above. Its oppositional transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Rain transforms by five. Below, it approaches the kidney’s *qi*; above, it follows the black *qi* ascending to serve heaven. Water changes to dust and obscurity, and the command of clouds and rain prevails. Damp *qi* triumphs, cold *qi* declines, and the kidney falls ill. Scaled creatures perish in disaster. When triumph is moderate, wood transforms and wind arrives. Dust flies through the great void, and sudden darkness arises. The people suffer from spleen illness, and scaled creatures perish in reverse. *Suixing* appears in the east at dusk, while *Zhenyao* appears small at dawn. This is called a *Heavenly Conformity* year for *Ji* earth, and its disasters are slightly reduced.

**Jiwei Year (6th Celestial Stem, 8th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *gong* phase prevails. *Taiyin* earth governs heaven, with dampness prevailing above. Its upright transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. *Ji* harmonizes with the *Heavenly Conformity* of earth. Rain transforms by five. The *qi* of transformation is damp and hot, the *qi* of the organs is warm in reverse, and the *qi* of growth aligns properly. Scaled creatures perish in disaster.

The kidneys store illness, and the people suffer from swelling and dampness above. Treat this with sour and balanced [remedies], using wood’s nature and wood’s flavor to balance earth’s power. *Zhenxing* appears large and flickering, while *Chenxing* is not seen.

**Gengyin Year (7th Celestial Stem, 3rd Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zheng* phase prevails. *Shaoyang* ministerial fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its upright transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Heat transforms by two, following the root’s generative number. The *qi* of growth issues fiery commands, the *qi* of harvest loses its mandate, and the *qi* of generation aligns properly. The lungs store illness, and scaled creatures perish in disaster. The people suffer from burning heat and vexing fullness above. Treat this with salty and cold [remedies], using water to subdue fire. *Yinghuo* appears at dusk, blazing brightly, while *Taibai* becomes the morning star at the fifth watch.

**Gengshen Year (7th Celestial Stem, 9th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *zheng* phase prevails. *Shaoyang* ministerial fire governs heaven, with heat prevailing above. Its oppositional transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Heat transforms by seven, following the branch’s completion number. Below, it overcomes kidney *qi*; above, it follows black *qi* in submission. Metal is activated, grasses and trees wither, fiery commands spread in season, and great heat melts metal. The lungs fall ill, scaled creatures perish in disaster, and autumn’s uprightness remains hot. When heat is extreme, cold water arrives in punishment—sudden chills strike abruptly, and the heart generates alternating cold and heat. Feathered creatures perish in loss, *Chenxing* appears early, and *Yinghuo* lingers at dusk. The year bears *Geng*, and though the lungs are endangered, they do not die; though afflicted, they do not suffer harm.

**Xinmao Year (8th Celestial Stem, 4th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. *Yangming* metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its oppositional transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Dryness transforms by nine, following the branch’s completion number. Below, it overcomes the liver’s stored *qi*; above, greenish *qi* submits to heaven. Earth then withers, dry *qi* frequently descends, and the liver stores illness while furred creatures perish in disaster. When its triumph is extreme, fiery heat spreads in flames, the lungs store illness in return, scaled creatures further decline, *Yinghuo* appears, and *Taibai* loses its luster.

**Xinyou Year (8th Celestial Stem, 10th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *shang* phase prevails. *Yangming* metal governs heaven, with dryness prevailing above. Its upright transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Dryness transforms by four, following the root’s generative number. The *qi* of harvest exerts clear dryness, the *qi* of generation loses its mandate, grasses and trees bloom late, and the *qi* of transformation aligns properly. *You* corresponds to metal, named *Heavenly Conformity*. The liver stores illness, furred creatures perish in disaster, and the people suffer from dryness above. Treat this with bitter and hot [remedies], using fire’s flavor and fire’s nature to subdue metal’s triumph. *Taibai* waxes greatly, while *Suixing* appears at dusk, small.

**Renchen Year (9th Celestial Stem, 5th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. *Taiyang* cold water governs heaven, with cold prevailing above. Its oppositional transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Cold transforms by six, following the branch’s completion number. Below, it overcomes the heart’s stored *qi*; above, red *qi* submits. Metal is about to flourish, and when cold’s essence rises in bleak seasons, great ice forms. Fire *qi* ascends in brilliance, the heart stores illness, and feathered creatures perish in disaster. When its triumph is extreme, earth and rain retaliate—scorching heat, dust, and dampness bring continuous downpours. The kidneys fall ill in return, scaled creatures suffer, *Chenxing* vanishes, and *Zhenxing* grows large and bright again.

**Renxu Year (9th Celestial Stem, 11th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *yu* phase prevails. *Taiyang* cold water governs heaven, with cold prevailing above. Its upright transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Cold transforms by one, following the root’s generative number. The *qi* of storage congeals in severity, the *qi* of growth loses its mandate, and the *qi* of harvest aligns properly. Below, the heart’s stored *qi* falls ill, and feathered creatures perish in disaster. The people suffer from cold above. Treat this with sweet and warm [remedies], using earth’s nature and earth’s flavor to subdue cold’s triumph. Do not consume salty and cold foods, lest they aid water’s triumph. *Chenxing* shines brightly, while *Yinghuo* dims.

**Guisi Year (10th Celestial Stem, 6th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. *Jueyin* wind-wood governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its oppositional transformation is abundant yet insubstantial, triumphant yet with retaliation. Wind transforms by eight, following the branch’s completion number. Below, it overcomes spleen *qi*; above, it follows yellowish *qi* in submission. Earth is about to flourish, water then withers, muscles grow heavy, and inner atrophy arises. The spleen stores illness, and armored creatures perish in disaster. When its triumph deepens, metal’s dryness arrives—stern killing arises, wood withers, the liver falls ill in return, and furred creatures perish in disaster. *Suixing* appears small, while *Taibai* shines brightly.

**Guihai Year (10th Celestial Stem, 12th Earthly Branch):**
Above, the upright *jiao* phase prevails. *Jueyin* wind-wood governs heaven, with wind prevailing above. Its upright transformation is abundant and substantial, triumphant yet without retaliation. Wind transforms by three, following the root’s generative number. The *qi* of generation flourishes, grasses and trees bloom early, the *qi* of transformation loses its mandate, and the *qi* of storage aligns properly. The spleen stores illness, and armored creatures perish in disaster. The people suffer from wind above. Treat this with acrid and cooling [remedies], using metal’s nature and metal’s flavor to subdue wind-wood’s triumph. Do not consume sour foods, lest they aid wood’s triumph. *Suixing* shines brightly, while *Zhenxing* dims.

**Completion of *Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu*, Scroll Four**

---

**Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu, Scroll Five**
*Qixuanzi’s Exposition*
*Divination of Qi and Yun: The Record of Cycles*

Movement is motion—circulation, recurrence, and revolution. Within the ascent and descent of the Great Void, above and below summon one another, and the signs of *qi* governing the turning of *yun* emerge.

Since the primordial beginning, when heaven and earth first parted, within the dual *qi* of ascent and descent, there has been the revolving, recurring *qi*, all endowed with the Five Phases. Thus, it is called the Five *Yun*. Specifically:
- Earth *yun* operates between *jia* and *ji*,
- Metal *yun* between *yi* and *geng*,
- Wood *yun* between *ding* and *ren*,
- Fire *yun* between *wu* and *gui*,
- Water *yun* between *bing* and *xin*.

Within these Ten Celestial Stems, the Five *Qi* circulate—this is called *yunqi*.

Within the second *jia* interval, within the governance of *Sitiān* and *Zaiquan*, it is thus named the Three Origins. When the Three Origins unite, movement begins. Thereupon, the Three Powers, the Four Seasons, and the Six *Qi*—all transformations and creations—arise from this.

Thus, some receive the heavenly mandate yet fail to transform; some punish earthly transformations yet fail to generate; some are subjected to heavenly governance yet the *yun* does not respond; some are borne by earth yet the *qi* is not concentrated. Some exceed and self-triumph; some fall short and suffer punishment from others; some self-deplete yet return to equilibrium. Therefore, the heavenly mandate responds to transformation, earthly products generate and complete, the Four Seasons alternate in correctness, and the myriad transformations wither and flourish—all arise from this.

Hence, auspicious omens and inauspicious portents become visible; peace and calamity may be foreknown; famine and abundance likewise depend on this; the people’s illnesses and disasters may also be verified.

Thus, the arrival has its day, observation has its time, and examination has its method. One must also divine by direction, calculate by position, and observe the hour—it cannot be perceived carelessly. It is necessary to scrutinize the days’ count, for there are inherent calculations of addition, subtraction, generation, completion, advance, and retreat.

One must also purify, fast, and abstain before observing—do not reveal this to the unworthy.

This method begins from the first day of the first month of the *jiazi* year of the first year of Linde in the Great Tang (a *jiyou* day), when the Metal Dog of *Lou* descended first. The accumulated years then subtract one; the next follows the sevenfold principle.

Next, divide by nineteen and subtract one—this is called the intercalary number. Then multiply by twelve, and after multiplying, add the intercalary number, followed by the number of the current month. Next, separately expand the lower position and then halve it. Then remove the intercalary number and further eliminate the Five Phases. Next, advance the upper position by one place and multiply by three. Then extract the number from the lower position—this is called "removing the lesser completion." Afterward, add the day under the month to determine the total. Then subtract sixty repeatedly; if there is a remainder, multiply it by one hundred. Again, subtract eighty-seven repeatedly; the remainder is then added to the *yun* number. If it exceeds, use the #3 completion number; if deficient, add the generative number to see the result.

In a yang year, if an even number is encountered, add one; in a yin year, if an odd number is encountered, subtract one. This number corresponds to the *ke* within the day. For excess *yun*, the twenty-four methods of all *yun* arrive on their appointed day; the qi *yun* arrives at its designated hour. Thus, excess arrives thirteen days early, deficiency arrives thirteen days late, balanced *qi yun* coincides with the ruling heaven on the same day, heavenly punishment *yun* arrives five days after the ruling heaven, and earthly punishment *yun* arrives six days after the ruling heaven. The calculations and methods have their own appointed times and hours.

1. *Jiazi*: *Jia* Earth *yun* in excess, *zi* as a yang year. The counting number increases by six—why? *Zi* belongs to *Kan*, its number is one; Earth *yun* has no completion number, so its number is five. Five and one together make six, thus adding six *ke* at the calculated hour. When the *yun* transitions, face *yin* and gaze forward. First, a green qi appears; once it fades, a yellow qi then flows horizontally from *jia* to *zi* and concludes. Its qi is deep and bright, with no other colors intermingling, signifying the abundance of the upper qi.

2. *Jiawu*: *Jia* Earth *yun* in excess, *wu* as a yang year. The counting number increases by fourteen—why? *Wu* belongs to *Li*, its number is nine; Earth’s number is five. Together they make fourteen, thus adding fourteen *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *yin* and gaze forward. First, a green-yellow qi appears; once it fades, a yellow qi then flows horizontally from *jia* to *wu* and concludes. Its qi moves swiftly and deeply, responding to the hour without other colors—this is auspicious, signifying the abundance of Earth qi.

3. *Jiaxu*: *Jia* Earth *yun* in excess, *xu* as a yang year. The counting number increases by ten—why? *Xu* belongs to Earth, its number is five; Earth *yun*’s number is also five. Two fives make ten, thus adding ten *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *yin* and gaze forward. First, a green qi appears; once it fades, a yellow qi then flows horizontally from *jia* to *xu* and concludes. It moves swiftly, its color deep, responding to the hour—this is auspicious; the opposite is inauspicious.

4. *Jiachen*: *Jia* Earth *yun* in excess, *chen* as a yang year. The counting number increases by ten *ke*—why? *Chen* belongs to Earth, its number is five; the *yun* is Earth, its number is also five. Two fives make ten, thus adding ten *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *yin* and gaze forward. First, a green qi appears; once it fades, a yellow qi then flows horizontally from *jia* to *chen* and concludes. Its qi is deep and swift, responding to the hour without shifting to other positions—all is auspicious.

5. *Jiashen*: *Jia* Earth *yun* in excess, *shen* as a yang year. The counting number increases by seven *ke*—why? *Shen* belongs to *Kun*, its number is two; Earth *yun*’s number is five. Two and five together make seven, thus adding seven *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *yin* and gaze forward. First, a green qi appears; once it fades, a yellow qi then flows horizontally from *jia* to *shen* and concludes. Its color responds to the hour without shifting, moving swiftly without straying—all is auspicious.

6. *Jiayin*: *Jia* Earth *yun* in excess, *yin* as a yang year. The counting number increases by thirteen—why? *Yin* belongs to *Gen*, its number is eight; Earth *yun*’s number is five. Eight and five together make thirteen, thus adding thirteen *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *yin* and gaze forward. First, a green qi appears; once it fades, a yellow qi emerges, rising upward without horizontal flow, as *yin* and *jia* share the same configuration. It does not shift with the hour, and its qi lingers long without dissipating—this is auspicious.

7. *Bingzi*: *Bing* Water *yun* in excess, *zi* as a yang year. The counting number increases by seven *ke*—why? *Zi* belongs to *Kan*, its number is one; Water *yun* in excess follows its completion number, six. One and six together make seven, thus adding seven *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *si* and gaze forward, as *bing* is lodged in the *si* position. First, a red qi appears; once it fades, a black qi then flows from *bing* to *zi* and concludes. Its qi is deep, swift, and timely, without shifting position—this is auspicious.

8. *Bingwu*: *Bing* Water *yun* in excess, *wu* as a yang year. The counting number increases by fifteen *ke*—why? *Wu* belongs to *Li*, its number is nine; Water *yun* in excess follows its completion number, six. Six and nine together make fifteen, thus adding fifteen *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *si* and gaze forward. First, a red qi appears; once it fades, a black qi then flows from *bing* to *wu*, all in black. The color appears alone, without shifting or encroaching on other positions—this is auspicious.

9. *Bingxu*: *Bing* Water *yun* in excess, *xu* as a yang year. The counting number increases by eleven—why? *Xu* belongs to Earth, its number is five; Water in excess follows its completion number, six. Five and six together make eleven, thus adding eleven *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *si* and gaze forward. First, a red qi appears; once it fades, a black qi then flows from *bing* to *xu* and concludes. Its qi is deep and swift, without encroaching on other colors—this is auspicious.

10. *Bingchen*: *Bing* Water *yun* in excess, *chen* as a yang year. The counting number increases by eleven—why?

*Chen* belongs to Earth, its number is five; Water in excess follows its completion number, six. Five and six together make eleven, thus adding eleven *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *si* and gaze forward. First, a red qi appears; once it fades, a black qi then flows from *bing* to *chen* and concludes. The black color arrives in timely sequence, without encroaching on other positions—this is auspicious.

11. *Bingshen*: *Bing* Water *yun* in excess, *shen* as a yang year. The counting number increases by eight—why? *Shen* belongs to *kun*, its number is two; Water in excess follows its completion number, six. Two and six together make eight, thus adding eight *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *si* and gaze forward. First, a red qi appears; once it fades, a black qi then flows from *bing* to *shen* and concludes. Its qi is deep and swift, arriving in timely sequence, without encroaching on other positions—this is auspicious.

12. *Bingyin*: *Bing* Water *yun* in excess, *yin* as a yang year. The counting number increases by fourteen—why? *Yin* belongs to *gen*, its number is eight; Water in excess follows its completion number, six. Eight and six together make fourteen, thus adding fourteen *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *si* and gaze forward. First, a red qi appears; once it fades, a black qi then flows from *bing* to *yin* and concludes. Its color is profound, swift in movement, arriving without missing its timely position—this is auspicious.

13. *Wuzi*: *Wu* Fire *yun* in excess, *zi* as a yang year. The counting number increases by eight—why? *Zi* belongs to *kan*, its number is one; Fire in excess follows its completion number, seven. Seven and one together make eight, thus adding eight *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *si* and gaze forward—both *bing* and *wu* reside in *si*. First, a yellow qi appears; once it fades, a red qi then flows from *wu* to *zi* and concludes. Its color is deep, its movement swift, arriving in timely sequence without shifting position—this is auspicious.

14. *Wuwu*: *Wu* Fire *yun* in excess, *wu* as a yang year. The counting number increases by sixteen—why? *Wu* belongs to *li*, its number is nine; Fire in excess follows its completion number, seven. Seven and nine together make sixteen, thus adding sixteen *ke*. When the *yun* transitions, face *si* and gaze forward. First, a yellow qi appears; once it fades, a red qi then flows from *wu* to *wu* and concludes. Its color is deep, its movement swift, returning to its original position in timely sequence—this is auspicious.

15. *Wushen*: *Wu* Fire *yun* in excess, *shen* as a yang year. The counting number increases by nine—why? *Shen* belongs to *kun*, its number is two; Fire in excess follows its completion number, seven. Two and seven together make nine, thus adding nine *ke*.
