Lesser Yin sovereign fire rules Heaven, and celestial *qi* revolves rightward, shifting three positions from *geng* to *wu*. *Wu* corresponds to *li*, its number nine; the metal phase being excessive, it follows the consummate number nine. Two nines combine to make eighteen. At the celestial hour, it arrives eighteen *ke* before the celestial count.

Three days later, fire begins to govern Heaven, initiating the celestial mandate. After nine days, *Tai Shang* submits to *Tai Zheng*. Red *qi* ascends, heat prevails in Heaven; yellow clouds appear in the east, green *qi* arises in the west—these are the signs of the two regulators’ alignment.

Black *qi* fills the sky, cold prevails above; in the east, green *qi* appears, while in the west, white dust emerges—these are the signs of the two regulators’ compliance.

Forty-sixth: In the *Ren-Xu* wood phase, the Northern Regulator governs Heaven; the celestial face turns south, with the left aligned to the east and the right to the west; above, *Tai-Yu* governs.
   The *Taiyang* Water governs Heaven; celestial *qi* revolves rightward, shifting two positions from *ren* to *xu*. *Xu* corresponds to earth, its number five; wood being excessive, it follows the completing number eight. Eight and five combine to make thirteen.
   Thirteen *ke* before the celestial count, the celestial timing arrives. Two days later, water begins to govern Heaven, initiating the celestial mandate. After eight days, Greater *Jue* harmonizes with *Tai-Yu*. Black *qi* fills the sky, cold prevails above; in the east, green *qi* arises, while in the west, white dust appears—these are the signs of the two regulators’ compliance.

Forty-seventh: In the *Gui-Si* fire phase, the Northern Regulator governs Heaven; the celestial face turns south, with the left aligned to the east and the right to the west; above, *Zheng-Jue* governs.
   The *Jueyin* Wood governs Heaven; celestial *qi* revolves rightward, shifting nine positions from *gui* to *si*. *Si* corresponds to *Xun*, its number four; fire being insufficient, it follows the generating number two. Two and four combine to make six.
   After six *ke* in the celestial count, the celestial timing arrives. Nine days later, wood begins to govern Heaven, initiating the celestial mandate. After fifteen days, Lesser *Zhi* harmonizes with *Zheng-Jue*. Green *qi* fills the sky, wind prevails above; in the east, red *qi* appears, while in the west, dusky dust emerges—these are the signs of the two regulators’ compliance.

Forty-eighth: In the *Gui-Hai* fire phase, the Northern Regulator governs Heaven; the celestial face turns south, with the left aligned to the east and the right to the west; above, *Tai-Jue* governs.
   The *Jueyin* Wood governs Heaven; celestial *qi* revolves rightward, shifting three positions from *gui* to *hai*. *Hai* corresponds to *Qian*, its number six; fire being insufficient, it follows the generating number two. Two and six combine to make eight.
   After eight *ke* in the celestial count, the celestial timing arrives. Three days later, wood begins to govern Heaven, initiating the celestial mandate. After fifteen days, Lesser *Zhi* harmonizes with *Tai-Jue*. Green *qi* fills the sky, wind prevails above; in the east, red *qi* appears, while in the west, black dust emerges—these are the signs of the two regulators’ compliance.

*Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu*, Scroll Eight, concludes.
*Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu*, Scroll Nine: *Qiyuanzi’s Exposition* begins.

**Celestial Governance and Cyclical Correspondences**

**Six Methods of Dominant Qi Governing Heaven**

1. *Bing-zi*: Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven; heat prevails above. The intermediary water phase is excessive, black *qi* surges to the sky, overwhelming celestial fire—its scorching mandate fails to manifest.

2. *Bing-wu*: Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven; heat prevails above. The intermediary water phase is excessive, black *qi* surges to the sky, overwhelming celestial fire—its transformative heat does not arise.

3. *Bing-yin*: Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven; heat prevails above. The intermediary water phase is excessive, black *qi* surges to the sky, overwhelming celestial fire—both summer heat and scorching mandates lose their transformation.

4. *Bing-shen*: Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven; heat prevails above. The intermediary water phase is excessive, black *qi* surges to the sky, overwhelming celestial fire—its transformative heat does not arise.

5. *Jia-xu*: Greater Yang Water governs Heaven; cold prevails above. The intermediary earth phase is excessive, yellow dust rises on all sides, overwhelming celestial water—cold transforms into dampness.

6. *Jia-chen*: Greater Yang Water governs Heaven; cold prevails above. The intermediary earth phase is excessive, yellow dust rises on all sides, overwhelming celestial water—cold fails to transform, instead generating dampness.

**Six Methods of Phase Qi Supporting Heaven**

1. *Yi-hai*: Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven; wind prevails above. The intermediary metal phase appears, white *qi* responds—metal restrains wood, and the wind mandate loses its efficacy. The term "supporting" denotes insufficiency in the phase, unlike excess; it thus tempers half the mandate.

2. *Yi-si*: Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven; wind prevails above. The intermediary metal phase appears, white *qi* responds—the wind mandate loses its efficacy.

3. *Gui-you*: Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven; dryness prevails above. The intermediary fire phase appears, red *qi* responds—the dryness mandate is tempered by half.

4. *Gui-mao*: Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven; dryness prevails above. The intermediary fire phase appears, red *qi* ascends—the dryness mandate loses its efficacy.

5. *Ding-wei*: Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven; dampness prevails above. The intermediary wood phase appears, green *qi* responds—the dampness mandate reverts to wind.

6. *Ding-chou*: Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven; dampness prevails above. The intermediary wood phase appears, green *qi* responds—the dampness mandate alternates with wind.

**Twelve Methods of Celestial Correspondences in Direct Alignment**

The term "direct" signifies alignment with Heaven; "correspondence" denotes union—thus, the heavenly stems unite with celestial governance.

1. *Bing-wu*: Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven. *Bing* is the fire stem of the southern quadrant. The stem aligns with the Celestial Dog; gazing afar into the great void, red *qi* ascends to the celestial horizon—its mandate unbroken, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue.

2. *Bing-zi*: Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven. *Bing* is the fire stem of the southern quadrant. The stem aligns with Heaven, red *qi* rising distantly to meet the celestial horizon.

3. *Yi-hai*: Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven. *Yi* is the wood position of the eastern quadrant. The wood stem harmonizes with celestial water, green *qi* like mist, lingering among the forests.

4. *Yi-si*: Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven. *Yi* is the wood stem of the eastern quadrant, aligning with Heaven’s virtue—above, it harmonizes with Heaven, while intermediary *qi* remains subtle.

5. *Ji-wei*: Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven. *Ji* is the earth stem of the central quadrant, aligning with Heaven above. Yellow *qi* arises from the cardinal directions, slightly aiding celestial *qi*.

6. *Ji-chou*: Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven. *Ji* is the earth stem of the central quadrant, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—slightly aiding Heaven.

7. *Xin-you*: Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven. *Xin* is the metal stem of the western quadrant, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—slightly aiding the intermediary mandate.

8. *Xin-mao*: Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven. *Xin* is the metal stem of the western quadrant, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—aligning with metal to assist.

9. *Ren-xu*: Greater Yang Water governs Heaven. *Ren* is the water stem of the northern quadrant, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—above, it aligns with celestial transformation, slightly aiding Heaven.

10. *Ren-chen*: Greater Yang Water governs Heaven. *Ren* is the water stem of the northern quadrant, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—above, it aligns with Heaven, slightly aiding its mandate.

11. *Bing-yin*: Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven. *Bing* is the fire stem of the southern quadrant, aligning with Heaven—slightly aiding Heaven’s mandate.

12. *Bing-shen*: Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven. *Bing* is the fire stem of the southern quadrant, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—slightly aiding Heaven.

**Twelve Methods of Phase Qi Harmonizing with Heaven**

1. *Ding-hai*: Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven. The intermediary wood phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—green *qi* ascends in unison, wind transformation aligns with its mandate. Heaven and phase mutually assist; *qi* transformation and mandate unite, above and center in accord.

2. *Ding-si*: Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven. The intermediary wood phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—green *qi* ascends in unison, wind transformation aligns with its mandate. Heaven and phase mutually assist; *qi* transformation is substantial, above and center free from restraint.

3. *Wu-zi*: Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven. The intermediary fire phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—red *qi* ascends in unison, heat transformation aligns with its mandate. Heaven and phase mutually assist; transformation is thus substantial.

4. *Wu-wu*: Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven. The intermediary fire phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—red *qi* ascends in unison, heat transformation aligns with its mandate. Heaven and phase mutually assist; their mandates unite as one.

5. *Yi-you*: Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven. The intermediary metal phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—white *qi* ascends in unison, dryness proceeds as one.

6. *Yi-mao*: Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven. The intermediary metal phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—white *qi* ascends in unison, dryness transformation aligns with its mandate.

7. *Ji-wei*: Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven. The intermediary earth phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—yellow *qi* ascends in unison, dampness transformation shares its mandate.

8. *Ji-chou*: Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven. The intermediary earth phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—yellow *qi* ascends in unison, its mandate aligning with Heaven’s. Rain and dampness transformations proceed as one.

9. *Bing-xu*: Greater Yang Water governs Heaven. The intermediary water phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—black *qi* ascends in unison, cold transformation shares its mandate.

10. *Bing-chen*: Greater Yang Water governs Heaven. The intermediary water phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—black *qi* ascends in unison, cold transformation shares its mandate.

11. *Wu-yin*: Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven. The intermediary fire phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—red *qi* ascends in offering, heat transformation aligns with its phase.

12. *Wu-shen*: Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven. The intermediary fire phase appears, harmonizing with Heaven’s virtue—red *qi* ascends in unison, heat transformation shares its mandate.

---

**Twelve Methods of Heaven Governing Below**

1. *Ji-hai*: Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven, with intermediary earth phase. Wood resides above, below it earth phase is deficient—phase declines, Heaven prevails. Green *qi* descends below, wind transformation overcomes rain.

2. *Ji-si*: Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven, with intermediary earth phase. Wood resides above, below it earth phase—Heaven restrains it. Wood *qi* descends below, green *qi* punishes yellow, wind transformation overcomes rain.

3. *Geng-zi*: Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary metal phase. Fire resides above, below it metal phase is deficient—red *qi* descends, metal *qi* fails to flourish, heat overcomes dryness.

4. *Geng-wu*: Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary metal phase. Fire resides above, below it metal *qi* is subdued by Heaven—red *qi* prevails below, metal cannot overcome it, heat and dryness unite in decline.

5. *Xin-wei*: Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven, with intermediary water phase. Earth resides above, below it water phase—cold transformation loses its mandate, yellow *qi* overcomes cold.

6. *Xin-chou*: Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven, with intermediary water phase. Earth resides above, below it water phase—water *qi* loses its mandate, beneath yellow *qi*, black *qi* is wholly subdued.

7. *Geng-shen*: Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary metal phase. Fire resides above, below it dry metal loses its mandate—beneath red *qi*, white dust is not manifest.

8. *Geng-yin*: Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary metal phase. Fire resides above, below it dry *qi*—severity is not enacted, scorching red *qi* prevails, metal’s mandate is deficient.

9. *Ding-you*: Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven, with intermediary wood phase. Metal resides above, below it wind transformation—dryness generates white *qi*, wood’s mandate returns in decline.

10. *Ding-mao*: Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven, with intermediary wood phase. Metal resides above, below it wind transformation—metal’s mandate enacts dryness, beneath white *qi*, wood’s mandate is deficient.

11. *Wu-xu*: Greater Yang Water governs Heaven, with intermediary fire phase. Water resides above, below it fire phase—heat’s mandate is untimely, beneath black *qi*, fire transformation cannot be enacted.

11. *Wu-chen*: Greater Yang Water governs Heaven, with water phase above, below it fire phase—heat transformation loses its season, cold transformation rules Heaven, summer’s mandate is wholly deficient.

---

**Twelve Methods of Harmonious Transformation Governing Heaven**

1. *Gui-hai*: Above, Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven, with intermediary fire phase—wood engenders fire. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath wood *qi*, fire phase serves Heaven.

2. *Gui-si*: Above, Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven, with intermediary fire phase—wood engenders fire. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath wood *qi*, fire phase serves Heaven.

3. *Jia-zi*: Above, Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary earth phase—fire engenders earth. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath fire *qi*, earth phase serves Heaven.

4. *Jia-wu*: Above, Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary earth phase—fire engenders earth. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath fire *qi*, earth phase serves Heaven.

5. *Yi-chou*: Above, Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven, with intermediary metal phase—earth engenders metal. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath earth *qi*, metal phase serves Heaven.

6. *Yi-wei*: Above, Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven, with intermediary metal phase—earth engenders metal. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath earth *qi*, metal phase serves Heaven.

7. *Jia-yin*: Above, Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary earth phase—fire engenders earth. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath fire *qi*, earth phase serves Heaven.

8. *Jia-shen*: Above, Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary earth phase—fire engenders earth. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath fire *qi*, earth phase serves Heaven.

9. *Xin-you*: Above, Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven, with intermediary water phase—metal engenders water. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath metal *qi*, water phase serves Heaven.

10. *Xin-mao*: Above, Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven, with intermediary water phase—metal engenders water. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath metal *qi*, water phase serves Heaven.

11. *Ren-xu*: Above, Greater Yang Water governs Heaven, with intermediary wood phase—water engenders wood. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath water *qi*, wood phase serves Heaven.

12. *Ren-chen*: Above, Greater Yang Water governs Heaven, with intermediary wood phase—water engenders wood. Father resides in the child’s position, thus it is harmonious. Beneath water *qi*, wood phase serves Heaven.

The twelve harmonious transformations governing Heaven all preside over auspiciousness; failure to serve Heaven results in misfortune.

---

**Twelve Methods of Reversed Transformation Governing Heaven**

1. *Xin-hai*: Above, Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven, with intermediary water phase—child wood resides above, father water below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath wood *qi*, water does not serve Heaven, thus it is inharmonious—hence a year of misfortune.

2. *Xin-si*: Above, Reverting Yin Wood governs Heaven, with intermediary water phase—child wood resides above, father water below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath wood *qi*, water does not serve Heaven, thus it is inharmonious—hence a year of misfortune.

3. *Ren-zi*: Above, Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary wood phase—child fire resides above, father wood below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath fire *qi*, wood does not serve Heaven, all reversed—hence a year of misfortune.

4. *Ren-wu*: Above, Lesser Yin Sovereign Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary wood phase—child fire resides above, father wood below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath fire *qi*, wood does not serve Heaven.

5. *Gui-chou*: Above, Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven, with intermediary fire phase—child earth resides above, father fire below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath earth *qi*, fire does not serve Heaven.

6. *Gui-wei*: Above, Greater Yin Earth governs Heaven, with intermediary fire phase—child earth resides above, father fire below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath earth *qi*, fire does not serve Heaven.

7. *Ren-yin*: Above, Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary wood phase—child fire resides above, father wood below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath fire *qi*, wood does not serve Heaven.

8. *Ren-shen*: Above, Lesser Yang Ministerial Fire governs Heaven, with intermediary wood phase—child fire resides above, father wood below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath fire *qi*, wood does not serve Heaven.

9. *Ji-you*: Above, Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven, with intermediary earth phase—child metal resides above, father earth below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath metal *qi*, earth does not serve Heaven.

10. *Ji-mao*: Above, Yang Brightness Metal governs Heaven, with intermediary earth phase—child metal resides above, father earth below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath metal *qi*, earth does not serve Heaven.

11. *Geng-xu*: Above, Greater Yang Water governs Heaven, with intermediary metal phase—child water resides above, father metal below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath water *qi*, metal does not serve Heaven.

12. *Geng-chen*: Above, Greater Yang Water governs Heaven, with intermediary metal phase—child water resides above, father metal below. Child resides in the father’s position, reversed. Beneath water *qi*, metal does not serve Heaven.

**Twelve Methods of Heavenly *Qi* Failing to Aid**

Whenever Heavenly *qi* fails to aid, it is because Heaven is deficient and intermediary *qi* arrives, or the phase’s *qi* is deficient and its conqueror arrives. Thus, Heavenly *qi* and the phase’s *qi* do not harmonize, each instead encountering its conqueror, leading to failure.

Each conqueror must seize its proper seasonal mandate to achieve mutual aid. From the three positions of *mao*, *si*, and *chou*—yin years of opposing transformations—twelve years are selected. Each position spans five years, from which three years of Heavenly *qi* aligning with virtue are chosen, yielding twelve years in total.

Excluded are:
- *Ding-si* phase, which aligns with Heaven as wood;
- *Ji-chou* phase, which aligns with Heaven as earth;
- *Yi-mao* phase, which aligns with Heaven as metal.

1. *Yi-si*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with left and right intermediary *qi* arriving from Heaven’s intervals. The phase’s metal is insufficient, and fire arrives to conquer. The phase is overcome by fire, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*—thus Heavenly *qi* cannot provide mutual aid.

2. *Ji-si*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s earth is insufficient, and wood arrives to conquer. The phase is punished by wood, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*—thus they do not aid one another.

3. *Gui-si*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s fire is insufficient, and water arrives to conquer. The phase is punished by water, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*—thus they do not aid one another.

4. *Xin-si*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s water is insufficient, and earth arrives to conquer. The phase is punished by earth, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*—thus Heaven and phase do not harmonize.

5. *Ding-mao*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s wood is insufficient, and metal arrives to conquer. Though the phase’s defeat is minor, Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*.

6. *Ji-mao*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s earth is insufficient, and wood arrives to conquer. The phase is overcome by wood, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*.

7. *Xin-mao*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s water is insufficient, and earth arrives to conquer. The phase is punished by earth, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*.

8. *Gui-mao*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s fire is insufficient, and water arrives to conquer. The phase is punished by water, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*.

9. *Ding-chou*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s wood is insufficient, and metal arrives to conquer. The phase is punished by metal, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*.

10. *Yi-chou*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s metal is insufficient, and fire arrives to conquer. The phase is punished by fire, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*.

11. *Xin-chou*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s water is insufficient, and earth arrives to conquer. The phase is punished by earth, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*.

12. *Gui-chou*: Heaven in opposing transformation, with intermediary *qi* arriving. The phase’s fire is insufficient, and water arrives to conquer. The phase is punished by water, and Heaven is invaded by intermediary *qi*.

*Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu*, Scroll Nine, concludes.

*Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu*, Scroll Ten
Attributed to Qixuanzi.

**Orthodox Transformations and Mandates: A Record**

**Thirty Methods of Orthodox Transformation Governing Heaven**

Orthodox transformation refers to the celestial mandate in its proper phase, its decree upright, free from perverse transformations, for the *qi* of Heaven is full.

1. *Yi-hai*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Wood’s root phase is *mao*, yet *mao* is opposed by the counter-phase of *yangming* metal. Wood is born in *hai*, hence the orthodox transformation. Orthodox transformation returns to its root, following the generative number three. After seventeen days of governing Heaven, the phase clashes above, and in the next three days, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, hibernating creatures perish, and the spleen repository ails. Five days later, yellow *qi* ascends, the upper *qi* slightly depleted, borne by the phase’s power. The mandate of wind transformation prevails, and though orthodox, metal’s phase slightly overcomes it, thus Heaven’s mandate is but a minor victory of wind.

2. *Ding-hai*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Wood returns to its root, following the generative number three. After sixteen days of governing Heaven, the phase arrives as above. In the next three days, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, hibernating creatures fail to thrive, and the ailment originates in the spleen. Five days later, yellow *qi* ascends, *shaogong* is subdued by *taijiao*, and green *qi* arrives in harmony. The mandate of orthodox transformation is full, prevailing without decline.

3. *Ji-hai*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Wood returns to its root, following the generative number three, with the phase’s number eight. After eight days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, hibernating creatures suffer calamity, the ailment originates in the spleen, and wind transforms. Eighteen days later, yellow *qi* ascends, *shaogong* arrives in subjugation, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, without decline.

4. *Xin-hai*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Wood returns to its root, following the generative number three, with the phase’s number four. After four days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, hibernating creatures fail to flourish, and the spleen repository ails. Seventeen days later, yellow *qi* ascends, *shaogong* resonates with *jiao*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, wind prevailing without decline.

5. *Gui-hai*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Wood returns to its root, following the generative number three, with the phase’s number five. After five days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, hibernating creatures are distressed, and the ailment originates in the spleen. Fifteen days later, yellow *qi* ascends, *shaogong* returns to resonate with *jiao*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, prevailing without decline.

6. *Jia-wu*: *Shaoyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following the generative number two, with the phase’s number seven. After seven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures fail to thrive, and the lung repository ails. Five days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* harmonizes with *zhengzhi*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, without decline.

7. *Bing-wu*: *Shaoyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following the generative number two, with the phase’s number eight. After eight days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures are afflicted, and the ailment originates in the lung. Six days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* returns to *taizhi*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, without decline.

8. *Wu-wu*: *Shaoyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following the generative number two, with the phase’s number nine. After nine days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures wither, and the lung ailment perishes. Seven days later, white *qi* ascends, the *shang* note returns to *zhi*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, without decline.

9. *Geng-wu*: *Shaoyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following the generative number two, with the phase’s number eleven. After eleven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook metal, yet metal is not subdued, only slightly weakened. Why? Metal is excessive, and Heaven’s victory is partial, hence it is not subdued. Armored creatures are slightly afflicted, and the lung ailment is mildly impaired. Nine days later, white *qi* ascends, *shang* does not return to *zhi*, yet the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, prevailing without decline.

10. *Ren-wu*: *Shaoyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following the generative number two, with the phase’s number ten. After ten days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures fail to thrive, and the lung ailment returns in affliction. Eight days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* partially harmonizes with *taizhi*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, without decline.

11. *Yi-wei*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Earth returns to its root, its number five, with the phase’s number nine. After nine days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is subdued, scaled creatures suffer disaster, and the kidney repository ails. Seventeen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* partially resides within *zhenggong*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation rains without cease.

12. *Ding-wei*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Earth returns to its root, its number five, with the phase’s number eight. After eight days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is subdued, scaled creatures fail to transform, and the kidney’s chronic ailment withers. Sixteen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* partially returns to *taigong*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, with dust and dampness intensifying.

13. *Ji-wei*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Earth returns to its root, its number five, with the phase’s number ten. After ten days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is subdued, scaled creatures fail to propagate, and the kidney repository declines. Seventeen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* is impaired, returning above to *zhenggong*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, with rain and dampness recurring.

14. *Xin-wei*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Earth returns to its root, its number five, with the phase’s number six. After six days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is slightly afflicted. Why? *Xin*’s water phase is overcome, and the day’s water begins to be subdued. Scaled creatures decline, and the kidney repository is afflicted. Fourteen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* partially harmonizes with *zhenggong*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, prevailing without decline.

15. *Gui-wei*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Earth returns to its root, its number five, with the phase’s number seven.

After seven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is subdued, scaled creatures suffer calamity, and kidney diseases prove fatal. Fifteen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* shifts to harmonize fully with *zhenggong*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, with clouds and rain recurring frequently.

16. *Jia-yin*: *Shaoyang* ministerial fire governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following its generative number two, with the phase’s number seven. After seven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, and armored creatures wither. Lung diseases relapse into decline. Five days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* shifts to harmonize with *zhengzhi*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, with scorching heat prevailing as the seasonal decree.

17. *Bing-yin*: *Shaoyang* ministerial fire governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following its generative number two, with the phase’s number eight. After eight days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures face peril, and lung diseases relapse into affliction. Six days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* shifts to harmonize fully with *zhengzhi*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, with intense heat prevailing unquestioned.

18. *Wu-yin*: *Shaoyang* ministerial fire governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following its generative number two, with the phase’s number nine. After nine days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, and armored creatures face peril. Seven days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* partially harmonizes with *taizhi*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, with scorching heat recurring frequently.

19. *Geng-yin*: *Shaoyang* ministerial fire governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following its generative number two, with the phase’s number eleven. After eleven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, the phase’s correspondence is slightly subdued, armored creatures are mildly afflicted, and lung diseases are not severe. Nine days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* does not harmonize with *zhi*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, with the decree of summer heat flourishing without decline.

20. *Ren-yin*: *Shaoyang* ministerial fire governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Fire returns to its root, following its generative number two, with the phase’s number ten. After ten days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures fail to transform, and lung diseases deepen. Eight days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* partially harmonizes with *zhengzhi*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full.

21. *Yi-you*: *Yangming* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Metal returns to its root, following its generative number four, with the phase’s number eight. After eight days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; wood is subdued, furred creatures perish, and liver diseases prove perilous. Seventeen days later, green *qi* ascends, the note *shaojiao* shifts and partially harmonizes with *zhengshang*, the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, and dryness enacts clear transformation.

22. *Ding-you*: *Yangming* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Metal returns to its root, following its generative number four, with the phase’s number seven. After seven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; wood is subdued, furred creatures are afflicted, and the liver repository suffers from pathogenic influence. Sixteen days later, green *qi* ascends, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, with dryness manifesting and wind diminishing.

23. *Ji-you*: *Yangming* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Metal returns to its root, following its generative number four, with the phase’s number nine. After nine days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; wood is subdued, furred creatures fall ill, and liver *qi* declines. Eighteen days later, green *qi* ascends, the note *shaojiao* returns to harmonize with *zhengshang*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, with dryness and clarity recurring frequently.

24. *Xin-you*: *Yangming* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Metal returns to its root, following its generative number four, with the phase’s number five. After five days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; wood is subdued, furred creatures suffer calamity, and liver *qi* fails to flourish. Fourteen days later, green *qi* ascends, the note *shaojiao* partially harmonizes with *zhengshang*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full.

25. *Gui-you*: *Yangming* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Metal returns to its root, following its generative number four, with the phase’s number six. After six days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; wood is subdued, furred creatures are afflicted, and the people suffer from liver repository diseases. Fourteen days later, green *qi* ascends, the note *shaojiao* harmonizes fully with *zhengshang*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation is full.

26. *Jia-xu*: *Taiyang* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Water returns to its root, following its generative number one, with the phase’s number six. After six days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; fire is subdued, feathered creatures suffer disaster, and the heart repository falls ill. Five days later, red *qi* ascends, the note *shaozhi* partially harmonizes with *zhengyu*, the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, and the decree of cold recurs.

27. *Bing-xu*: *Taiyang* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Water returns to its root, following its generative number one, with the phase’s number seven. After seven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; fire is subdued, feathered creatures suffer disaster, and the heart repository falls ill. Six days later, red *qi* ascends, the note *shaozhi* partially harmonizes with *zhengyu*, and the mandate of cold transformation prevails.

28. *Wu-xu*: *Taiyang* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Water returns to its root, following its generative number one, with the phase’s number eight. After eight days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; fire is subdued, feathered creatures fall ill, and the heart repository declines. Seven days later, red *qi* ascends, the note *shaozhi* partially harmonizes with *zhengyu*, the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, and cold clouds prevail as the seasonal decree.

29. *Geng-xu*: *Taiyang* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Water returns to its root, following its generative number one, with the phase’s number ten. After ten days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; fire is subdued, feathered creatures suffer calamity, and the heart repository falls ill. Nine days later, red *qi* ascends, the note *shaozhi* partially harmonizes with *zhengyu*, the mandate of orthodox transformation is full, and the decree of cold transformation prevails as the seasonal decree.

30. *Ren-xu*: *Taiyang* governs Heaven in orthodox transformation. Water returns to its root, following its generative number one, with the phase’s number nine. After nine days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; fire is subdued, feathered creatures suffer disaster, and the heart repository falls ill. Eight days later, red *qi* ascends, the note *shaozhi* partially harmonizes with *zhengyu*, and the mandate of orthodox transformation remains full without decline.

*Dui Si Yi Zheng Ji Pian* concludes.

**Thirty Methods of Opposing Transformation Governing Heaven**

Opposing transformation refers to the transformation of opposing positions in opposition. In opposing transformation, Heaven’s emptiness alters its orthodox mandate, and the numbers follow completion.

1. *Yi-si*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Wood opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number eight. Below, it encounters metal’s *qi*, and the phase’s number is not communicated. After eight days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, armored creatures suffer disaster, and the spleen repository falls ill. Twenty-one days later, yellow *qi* ascends, the note *shaogong* does not return to the orthodox *jiao*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full. Wind contains dryness, thus within wind’s transformation, dryness interposes.

2. *Ding-si*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Wood opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number eight, with the phase’s number eleven. After eleven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, armored creatures perish, and the spleen dies of illness. Sixteen days later, yellow *qi* ascends, the note *shaogong* does not return to the orthodox *jiao*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full. Heaven’s mandate flourishes yet contains decline, and the mandate loses its orthodoxy.

3. *Ji-si*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Wood opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number eight, with the phase’s number thirteen. After thirteen days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, extraordinary creatures fall ill, and the spleen repository weakens. Eighteen days later, yellow *qi* ascends, the note *shaogong* does not return to the orthodox *jiao*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

4. *Xin-si*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Wood opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number eight, with the phase’s number nine. After nine days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, armored creatures fail to reproduce, and the spleen repository falls ill. Fourteen days later, yellow *qi* ascends, the note *shaogong* does not return to the orthodox *jiao*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

5. *Gui-si*: *Jueyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Wood opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number eight, with the phase’s number ten. After ten days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; earth is subdued, armored creatures fail to thrive, and the spleen falls ill. Fifteen days later, yellow *qi* ascends, the note *shaogong* does not return to the orthodox *jiao*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

6. *Jia-zi*: *Shaoyin* sovereign fire governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Fire opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number seven, with the phase’s number twelve. After twelve days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, scaled creatures fall ill, and the lung repository suffers punishment. Nine days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *taishang* does not return to the orthodox *zheng*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

7. *Bing-zi*: *Shaoyin* sovereign fire governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Fire opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number seven, with the phase’s number thirteen. After thirteen days of governing Heaven, white *qi* ascends, the note *taishang* does not return to the orthodox *zheng*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

8. *Wu-zi*: *Shaoyin* sovereign fire governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Fire opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number seven, with the phase’s number fourteen. After fourteen days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, scaled creatures are distressed, and those with a fundamentally weak lung repository die. Seven days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *taishang* does not return to the orthodox *zheng*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

9. *Geng-zi*: *Shaoyin* sovereign fire governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Fire opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number seven, with the phase’s number sixteen. After sixteen days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is slightly subdued, and the phase is excessively full—why is this? Scaled creatures are mildly ill, and the lung is slightly diseased. Nine days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *taishang* does not return to the orthodox *zheng*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

10. *Ren-zi*: *Shaoyin* sovereign fire governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Fire opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number seven, with the phase’s number fifteen. After fifteen days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, scaled creatures fall ill, and the lung repository weakens. Six days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *taishang* does not govern the orthodox *zheng*, flourishing yet not full, prevailing yet returning to decline.

11. *Yi-chou*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Earth opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number five, with the phase’s number nine. After nine days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is subdued, scaly creatures fail to propagate, and the kidney repository falls ill. Seventeen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* does not return to the orthodox *gong*, flourishing yet not full, prevailing yet returning to decline.

12. *Ding-chou*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Earth opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number five, with the phase’s number eight. After eight days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is subdued, and scaly creatures fall ill. Sixteen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* does not return to the orthodox *gong*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

13. *Ji-chou*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Earth opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number five, with the phase’s number ten. After ten days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is subdued, scaly creatures fall ill, and the kidney dies of illness. Eighteen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* does not return to the orthodox *gong*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

14. *Xin-chou*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Earth opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number five, with the phase’s number six. After six days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is subdued, scaly creatures suffer calamity, and the kidney falls ill. Fourteen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* does not return to the orthodox *gong*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

15. *Gui-chou*: *Taiyin* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Earth opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number five, with the phase’s number seven. After seven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; water is subdued, scaly creatures fail to reproduce, and the kidney weakens.

Fifteen days later, black *qi* ascends, the note *shaoyu* does not return to the orthodox *gong*, flourishing yet not full, prevailing yet returning to decline.

16. *Jia-shen*: *Shaoyang* Ministerial Fire governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Fire opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number seven, with the phase’s number twelve. After twelve days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures fall ill, and the lung weakens. Five days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* does not return to *taizhi*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

17. *Bing-shen*: *Shaoyang* Ministerial Fire governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Fire opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number seven, with the phase’s number thirteen. After thirteen days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures suffer distress, and the lung falls ill. Six days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* does not return to *taizhi*, flourishing yet not full, prevailing yet returning to decline.

After fourteen days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures suffer distress, and the lung weakens. Five days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* does not return to *taizhi*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

After sixteen days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures suffer calamity, and the lung falls gravely ill. Nine days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* does not return to *taizhi*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

20. *Ren-shen*: *Shaoyang* Ministerial Fire governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Fire opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number seven, with the phase’s number fifteen. After fifteen days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; metal is subdued, armored creatures fall ill, and the lung weakens. Eight days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaoshang* does not return to *taizhi*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

21. *Yi-mao*: *Yangming* governs Heaven in opposing transformation. Metal opposes and transforms in its position, following its completion number nine, with the phase’s number thirteen. After thirteen days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; wood is subdued, furred creatures suffer distress, and the liver falls mortally ill. Seventeen days later, green *qi* ascends, the note *shaojiao* does not return to the orthodox *shang*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

After twelve days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; wood is subdued, furred creatures fall ill, and the liver weakens. Sixteen days later, green *qi* ascends, the note *shaojiao* does not return to the orthodox *shang*, flourishing yet not full, prevailing yet returning to decline.

Eighteen days later, green *qi* ascends, the note *shaojiao* does not return to the orthodox *shang*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

After ten days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; wood is subdued, furred creatures fall ill, and the liver’s *qi* weakens. Fourteen days later, green *qi* ascends, the note *shaojiao* does not return to the orthodox *shang*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

After eleven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; wood is subdued, furred creatures suffer distress, and the liver falls ill. Three days later, white *qi* ascends, the note *shaojiao* does not return to the orthodox *shang*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

After eleven days of governing Heaven, it descends to overlook; fire is subdued, feathered creatures fail to reproduce, and the heart falls ill. Six days later, red *qi* ascends, the note *shaozhi* does not return to *taiyu*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

After eight days, red *qi* ascends, the note *shaozhi* does not return to *taiyu*, flourishing yet returning to decline, prevailing yet not full.

*Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu*, Scroll Ten, concludes.

---

*Suwen Liuqi Xuanzhu Miyu*, Scroll Eleven
*Qixuanzi’s Exposition*
*Annals of Intercalary Governance Between Heaven*

**Thirty-Six Methods of Major and Minor Intercalary Governance Between Heaven**

1. *Jia-zi*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial timing follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then proceeds to the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right.

*Intercalation* refers to the left and right following the commands of governance, deferring to Heaven’s decree—yet Heaven’s decree does not self-correct its transformation.

2. *Bing-zi*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

3. *Wu-zi*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven, its decree aligning with fire—this is *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When the year follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

4. *Geng-zi*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering is odd, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when even, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

5. *Ren-zi*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; Wood phase assists Heaven—this is Wood generating Fire, hence *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering is odd, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when even, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

6. *Yi-chou*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering is odd, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when even, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

7. *Ding-chou*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase restrains Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

8. *Ji-chou*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven, Earth phase aligning with Heaven above—this is *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering is odd, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when even, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

9. *Xin-chou*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering is odd, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when even, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

10. *Gui-chou*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven—this is Fire generating Earth, hence *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering is odd, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when even, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

11. *Yi-mao*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven, Metal phase aligning with Heaven’s decree above—this is *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

12. *Ding-mao*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

13. *Ji-mao*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven—this is Earth generating Metal, hence *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

14. *Xin-mao*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

15. *Gui-mao*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

16. *Jia-chen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

17. *Bing-chen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven—Water aligns with Heaven’s decree, hence *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

18. *Wu-chen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

19. *Geng-chen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven—Metal generates Water, hence *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

20. *Ren-chen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated.

When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

21. *Yi-si*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

22. *Ding-si*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven, as Wood aligns with Heaven’s decree—this is *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

23. *Ji-si*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

24. *Xin-si*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven, as Water generates Wood—this is *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

25. *Gui-si*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

26. *Jia-shen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

27. *Bing-shen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

28. *Wu-shen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase assists Heaven, as Fire aligns with Heaven’s decree—this is *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

29. *Geng-shen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

30. *Ren-shen*: Opposing transformation renders Heaven vacuous; the phase does not assist Heaven—this is *major intercalation*, wherein both left and right are intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, it first intercalates the left, then the right; when following an even number, it first intercalates the right, then the left.

Opposing transformation encompasses thirty instances, which include both major and minor intercalations. Why then are thirty-six mentioned? Six years are extracted from the *proper transformation*, comprising three years of *overcoming* phases and three years of *compliance* phases—altogether six years. These are also *minor intercalations*, though even more subtle.

31. *Bing-wu*: Though within *proper transformation*, Water phase overcomes Heaven, and Heaven’s decree is not upright—thus a *minor vacuity*, also a *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

32. *Bing-yin*: Though within *proper transformation*, Water phase overcomes Heaven, and Heaven’s decree is not upright—thus a *minor vacuity*, also a *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

33. *Jia-xu*: Though within *proper transformation*, Earth phase overcomes Heaven, and Heaven’s decree is not upright—thus a *minor vacuity*, also a *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

34. *Yi-hai*: Though within *proper transformation*, Metal phase complies with Heaven, and Heaven’s decree is not upright—thus a *minor vacuity*, also a *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

35. *Gui-you*: Though within *proper transformation*, Fire phase complies with Heaven, and Heaven’s decree is not upright—thus a *minor vacuity*, also a *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

36. *Ding-wei*: Though within *proper transformation*, Wood phase complies with Heaven, and Heaven’s decree is not upright—thus a *minor vacuity*, also a *minor intercalation*, wherein only one side is intercalated. When celestial numbering follows an odd number, the left is intercalated and the right is not; when following an even number, the right is intercalated and the left is not.

*Plain Questions: Six Qi Mysterious Pearl Secret Sayings*, Scroll Eleven, concludes.

*Plain Questions: Six Qi Mysterious Pearl Secret Sayings*, Scroll Twelve
By Master Qi Xuan

**Three Origins Matched with Cyclical Revolutions: Proper Transformations in the Subterranean Springs, Thirty Methods**

1. *Jia-wu*: Oppose and take the subterranean *jia-zi*; one should see *ji-you*. Thus, celestial *jia-zi* is *jia*, and terrestrial *jia-zi* is *ji*. *Jia* and *ji* unite—this is the pairing of Heaven and Earth. Therefore, when *jia* is in Heaven, *ji* is on Earth. Within the interval of *jia* and *ji*, the Earth phase arises. Thus, celestial *jia-zi* is *jia-wu*, and terrestrial *jia-zi* is *ji-you*. The terrestrial *jia-zi* departs from the celestial *jia-zi* by fifteen days, below manifesting *yangming* Metal’s proper transformation in the subterranean springs. Fifteen days after the celestial controller’s succession, Earth’s transition occurs—this is *Lichun*. It also follows celestial numbering: after the celestial controller’s succession by 1,500 *ke*, Earth’s transition occurs. Thus, *you* is *dui*, its number seven; *ji* is Earth, its number five. Seven and five complete twelve—twelve *ke* after Earth’s transition, Metal enters the Earth. From *ji* to *you*, proceeding three positions, three days after Earth’s transition, Metal begins to govern the Earth. *Xin* entities then arise, and Earth’s *qi* becomes dry. After seven days, white *qi* descends and generates; Earth’s *qi* submits to the revolution.

2. *Bing-wu*: This is celestial *jia-zi*, below manifesting *xin-you*, terrestrial *jia-zi*. It departs by fifteen positions from the previous. *Bing* is in Heaven, *xin* on Earth. Within the interval of *bing* and *xin*, the Water phase arises. Thus, Earth sees *xin-you*, *yangming*’s proper transformation in the subterranean springs. Thus, *you* is *dui*, its number seven; *xin* is the Water phase, its number one. One and seven complete eight—eight *ke* after Earth’s transition, Metal enters the Earth. From *xin* to *you*, proceeding twelve positions, twelve days after Earth’s transition, Metal begins to govern the Earth. *Xin* entities then arise, and Earth’s *qi* becomes dry. After seven days, white *qi* descends and generates; Earth’s *qi* submits to the revolution.

3. *Wu-wu*: This is celestial *jia-zi*, below manifesting *gui-you*, terrestrial *jia-zi*. Thus, celestial *wu* and terrestrial *gui*. Within the interval of *wu* and *gui*, the Fire phase arises. Thus, Earth sees *gui-you*, *yangming*’s proper transformation in the subterranean springs. Thus, *you* is *dui*, its number seven; *gui* is the Fire phase, its number two. Two and seven complete nine—nine *ke* after Earth’s transition, it arrives. From *gui* to *you*, proceeding nine positions, nine days after Earth’s transition, Metal begins to govern the Earth. *Xin* entities then arise, and dryness prevails on Earth. After seven days, white *qi* descends, and Metal’s *qi* submits to the revolution.

4. *Geng-wu*: This is celestial *jia-zi*, below manifesting *yi-you*, terrestrial *jia-zi*. Thus, celestial *geng* and terrestrial *yi*. Within the interval of *yi* and *geng*, the Metal phase arises. Thus, Earth sees *yi-you*, *yangming*’s proper transformation in the subterranean springs. Thus, *you* is *dui*, its number seven; *yi* is the Metal phase, its number four. Four and seven complete eleven—eleven *ke* after Earth’s transition, Metal enters the Earth. From *yi* to *you*, proceeding six positions, six days after Earth’s transition, Metal begins to govern the Earth. *Xin* entities then arise, and dryness prevails on Earth. After seven days, white *qi* descends, and Earth’s *qi* submits to the revolution.

5. *Ren-wu*: This is celestial *jia-zi*, below manifesting *ding-you*, terrestrial *jia-zi*. Thus, celestial *ren* and terrestrial *ding*. Within the interval of *ding* and *ren*, the Wood phase arises. Thus, Earth sees *ding-you*, *yangming*’s proper transformation in the subterranean springs. Thus, *you* is *dui*, its number seven; *ding* is the Wood phase, its number three. Three and seven complete ten—ten *ke* after Earth’s transition, Metal enters the Earth. From *ding* to *you*, proceeding three positions, three days after Earth’s transition, Metal begins to govern the Earth. *Xin* entities then arise, and dryness prevails on Earth. After seven days, white *qi* descends, and Metal’s *qi* submits to the revolution.

6. *Yi-wei*: This is celestial *jia-zi*, below manifesting *geng-xu*, terrestrial *jia-zi*. Thus, celestial *yi* and terrestrial *geng*. Within the interval of *yi* and *geng*, the Metal phase arises. Thus, Earth sees *geng-xu*, *taiyang* in the subterranean springs. Thus, *xu* is Earth, its number five; *geng* is the Metal phase, its number nine. Five and nine complete fourteen—fourteen *ke* before Earth’s transition, it arrives. From *geng* to *xu*, proceeding three positions, three days after Earth’s transition, Water begins to govern the Earth. Saline entities then arise, and cold prevails on Earth. After five days, black *qi* descends and generates; Earth’s *qi* submits to the revolution.

7. *Ding-wei*: This is celestial *jia-zi*, below manifesting *ren-xu*, terrestrial *jia-zi*. Thus, celestial *ding* and terrestrial *ren*. Within the interval of *ding* and *ren*, the Wood phase arises. Thus, Earth sees *ren-xu*, *taiyang*’s proper transformation in the subterranean springs. Thus, *xu* is Earth, its number five; *ren* is Wood, its number eight. Eight and five complete thirteen—thirteen *ke* before Earth’s transition, Water enters the Earth. From *ren* to *xu*, proceeding twelve positions, twelve days after Earth’s transition, Water begins to govern the Earth. Saline entities then arise, and cold prevails on Earth. After five days, black *qi* descends, and Earth’s *qi* submits to the revolution.

8. *Ji-wei*: This is celestial *jia-zi*, below manifesting *jia-xu*, terrestrial *jia-zi*. Thus, celestial *ji* and terrestrial *jia*. Within the interval of *jia* and *ji*, the Earth phase arises. Thus, Earth sees *jia-xu*, *taiyang*’s proper transformation in the subterranean springs. Thus, *xu* is Earth, its number five; *jia* is the Earth phase, its number five. Two fives complete ten—ten *ke* before Earth’s transition, Water begins to enter the Earth. From *jia* to *xu*, proceeding nine positions, nine days after Earth’s transition, Water begins to govern the Earth. Saline entities then arise. After five days, black *qi* descends, and Earth’s *qi* submits to the revolution.

9. *Xin-wei*: This is celestial *jia-zi*, below manifesting *bing-xu*, terrestrial *jia-zi*. Thus, celestial *xin* and terrestrial *bing*. Within the interval of *bing* and *xin*, the Water phase arises. Thus, Earth sees *bing-xu*, *taiyang*’s proper transformation in the subterranean springs.

Thus, Earth sees *wu-xu*, *taiyang*’s proper transformation in the subterranean springs. Thus, *xu* is Earth, its number five; *wu* is the Fire phase, its number seven. After six days, green mist descends, and Earth’s *qi* submits to the revolution.

*Plain Questions: Six Qi Mysterious Pearl Secret Sayings*, Scroll Twelve, concludes.
*Plain Questions: Six Qi Mysterious Pearl Secret Sayings*, Scroll Thirteen, as recorded by Qi Xuanzi.

**Earth’s Correspondence to the Three Yuan Cycles: Thirty Methods of Transformation in the Subterranean Springs**

1. *Jiazi*: Heaven’s *jiazi*, below appears *jimao*, Earth’s *jiazi*. Thus, Heaven is *jia* and Earth is *ji*. Within the interval of *jia* and *ji*, the Earth phase arises. Here, Earth sees *jimao*, *yangming* Ministerial Metal in its proper transformation within the subterranean springs—Metal in opposition to its position. Thus, *mao* is *zhen*, its number three; *ji* is the Earth phase, its number five. Three and five complete eight—eight *ke* before Earth’s transition, Metal enters the Earth. From *ji* to *mao*, proceeding leftward five positions. Five days after Earth’s transition, Metal begins to govern the Earth. Dryness pervades the Earth, and acrid entities arise. After three days, the *qi* of the phase and the revolution descend together, and intermediary entities arise in unison.

2. *Bingzi*: Heaven’s *jiazi*, below appears *xinmao*, Earth’s *jiazi*. Thus, Heaven is *bing* and Earth is *xin*. Within the interval of *bing* and *xin*, the Water phase arises. Here, Earth sees *xinmao*, *yangming* Ministerial Metal in its proper transformation within the subterranean springs—Metal in opposition to its position. Thus, *mao* is *zhen*, its number three; *xin* is the Water phase, its number one. One and three complete four—four *ke* before Earth’s transition, Metal enters the Earth. From *xin* to *mao*, proceeding leftward eight positions. Eight days after Earth’s transition, Metal begins to govern the Earth. Dryness pervades the Earth, and acrid entities arise. After three days, the *qi* of the phase and the revolution descend together, and intermediary entities arise in unison.

3. *Wuzi*: Heaven’s *jiazi*, below appears *guimao*, Earth’s *jiazi*. Thus, Heaven is *wu* and Earth is *gui*. Within the interval of *wu* and *gui*, the Fire phase arises. Here, Earth sees *guimao*, *yangming* Ministerial Metal in its proper transformation within the subterranean springs. Thus, *mao* is *zhen*, its number three; *gui* is the Fire phase, its number two. Two and three complete five—five *ke* after Earth’s transition, Metal enters the Earth. From *gui* to *mao*, proceeding leftward eleven positions. Eleven days after Earth’s transition, Metal begins to govern the Earth. Dryness pervades the Earth, and acrid entities arise. After three days, the *qi* of the phase and the revolution descend together, and intermediary entities arise in unison.

4. *Gengzi*: Heaven’s *jiazi*, below appears *yimao*, Earth’s *jiazi*. Thus, Heaven is *geng* and Earth is *yi*. Within the interval of *yi* and *geng*, the Metal phase arises. Here, Earth sees *yimao*, *yangming* Ministerial Metal in its proper transformation within the subterranean springs. Thus, *mao* is *zhen*, its number three; *yi* is the Metal phase, its number four. Four and three complete seven—seven *ke* after Earth’s transition, Metal enters the Earth. From *yi* to *mao*, proceeding leftward one position. One day after Earth’s transition, Metal begins to govern the Earth. Dryness pervades the Earth, and acrid entities arise. After three days, the *qi* of the phase and the revolution descend together, and intermediary entities arise in unison.

Here, Earth sees *dingmao*, *yangming* Ministerial Metal in its proper transformation within the subterranean springs. Thus, *mao* is *zhen*, its number three; *ding* is the Wood phase, its number three. Two and three complete six—six *ke* after Earth’s transition, Wood enters the Earth. From *ding* to *mao*, proceeding leftward five positions. Five days after Earth’s transition, Wood begins to govern the Earth. Dryness pervades the Earth, and acrid entities arise.
