In *zi* and *wu* yang years, excess should yield *Greater Jue*, yet here it is *Lesser Jue*—why? *Wu* is Fire, and Wood encounters Fire in weakness, thus *ren-wu* is *Lesser Jue*, while *ren-zi* is *Greater Jue*, giving rise to these two interpretations. This is the Fifth Origin of Nourishment.

*Greater Zhi* arises when *ren-wu* gives birth to *gui-wei*, and *ren-zi* gives birth to *gui-chou*. *Gui* originally resides in *chou*, but when the heavenly stem aligns with the direct agent, it becomes *Greater Zhi*. Thus, from the head *wu* to the tail *gui*, *wu* and *gui* unite in the Fire phase—this completes the cycle of the Primordial Origin.

*Lesser Yang* governs heaven, and Earth phase prevails as *Lesser Yang*, hence this is the Second [cycle]. *Greater Gong* appears as the central Earth phase. *Jueyin* Wood is in the spring below, and Earth is overcome by the phase of the land.

In *jia-yin* and *jia-shen* years, *yin* governs direct transformation, while *shen* governs oppositional transformation. Its phase is yin rain, and the Earth phase enacts the rain mandate to transform. Its transformations are softness, moisture, and heavy marsh—*ji* transforms into dampness, and the seasonal mandate is damp-heat. Thus, when all things are overly soft and moist, prolonged rain and deep yin are called "heavy marsh."

Its excesses are trembling, fright, whirlwinds, and sudden fury—manifesting as sudden collapse and unceasing diarrhea, termed "excessive transformation." Its afflictions are heavy body, edema, glomus, and phlegm-rheum. Excess leads to spleen disorders, and prolonged harm extends to the kidneys.

*Greater Gong* corresponds to *jia-yin* and *jia-shen*. *Jia* governs the Earth phase, and *Gong* is the Earth tone.

In *yin* and *shen* yang years, as yang years are excessive, they correspond to *Greater Gong*. This is the first *yuan*. *Greater Shang* arises from *jia-yin* generating *yi-mao*, and *jia-shen* generating *yi-you*. *Yi* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone. *Mao* and *you* are yin years of insufficiency, which should correspond to *Lesser Shang*; why then is it *Greater Shang*? This is because *Yangming* Metal appears above, and the phase aligns with the celestial tally. This is the second *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Greater Yu* concludes with *yi-mao* generating *bing-chen*, and *yi-you* generating *bing-xu*. *Bing* governs the Water phase, and *Yu* is the Water tone. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years of excess, hence *Greater Yu*. This is the third *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Greater Jue* arises from *bing-chen* generating *ding-si*, and *bing-xu* generating *ding-hai*. *Ding* governs the Wood phase, and *Jue* is the Wood tone. *Si* and *hai* are yin years, which should correspond to *Lesser Jue*; why then is it *Greater Jue*? This is because the Earth phase encounters *Jueyin* Wood as the celestial controller, aligning with Wood. This is the fourth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Greater Zhi* arises from *ding-si* generating *wu-wu*, and *ding-hai* generating *wu-zi*. *Wu* governs the Fire phase, and *Zhi* is the Fire tone. *Zi* and *wu* are yang years, inherently excessive, hence *Greater Zhi*. This is the fifth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Lesser Gong* arises from *wu-zi* generating *ji-chou*, and *wu-wu* generating *ji-wei*. Beginning with *jia* and ending with *ji*, it completes the Earth phase. This is the sixth *yuan*, returning full circle to the beginning.

*Shaoyang* governs the heavens, and as Metal phase meets *Shaoyang*, it is designated the fourth. *Greater Shang* corresponds to the Metal phase. Below, *Jueyin* Wood resides in the springs, where Metal phase overcomes Earth’s Wood. *Geng-yin* and *geng-shen* enact direct transformation in *yin*, and oppositional transformation in *shen*. Its phase is frozen Metal, and the Metal phase enacts the freezing mandate to transform. Its transformations are mist, dew, and crystalline clarity—Metal in excess stirs white dust on all sides, transforming into mist and dew. *Crystalline clarity* reflects Metal’s pure and resonant nature.

Its excesses are stern desiccation and withering decay—excesses that deviate from the norm. Metal’s wrath manifests as white *qi* transforming into killing force, causing grasses and trees to wither prematurely, not awaiting their yellowing. Its afflictions are the shoulders, back, and chest; excess harms the lungs, and prolonged harm extends to the liver.

*Lesser Shang* corresponds to *geng-yin* and *geng-shen*. *Geng* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone.

In *yin* and *shen* yang years, they should correspond to *Tai Shang*, yet they instead manifest as *Shao Shang*—why is this? It is because *Shao Yang* ministerial fire presides over heaven above, and heavenly fire restrains them, hence the name *heavenly punishment*. Thus, under *Shao Shang*, all transformative mandates from *si* onward do not align.

*Shao Yu* concludes with *geng-yin* generating *xin-mao*, and *geng-shen* generating *xin-you*. *Xin* governs the water phase, and *Yu* is the water tone. *Mao* and *you* are yin years of insufficiency, hence *Shao Yu*. This is the second *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Jue* begins with *xin-mao* generating *ren-chen*, and *xin-you* generating *ren-xu*. *Ren* governs the wood phase, and *Jue* is the wood tone. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Jue*. This is the third *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Zhi* follows with *ren-chen* generating *gui-si*, and *ren-xu* generating *gui-hai*. *Gui* governs the fire phase, and *Zhi* is the fire tone. *Si* and *hai* are yin years, which should be insufficient and thus *Shao Zhi*—yet they manifest as *Tai Zhi*. Why? Because *si* is fire, and here it aligns with the yearly branch, hence *Tai Zhi*. Thus, *si* is *Tai* while *hai* is *Shao*—these are the two explanations. This is the fourth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Gong* follows with *gui-si* generating *jia-wu*, and *gui-hai* generating *jia-zi*. *Jia* governs the earth phase, and *Gong* is the earth tone. *Zi* and *wu* are yang years, hence *Tai Gong*. This is the fifth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Shang* follows with *jia-wu* generating *yi-wei*, and *jia-zi* generating *yi-chou*. *Yi* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone. Here, *geng* begins and *yi* concludes—*yi* meets *geng* to harmonize its Metal, thus *Shang* returns and restores. As *Shao Yang* presides over heaven, water returns to *Shao Yang*, hence the fifth position.

*Tai Yu* is centered in the water phase. *Jue Yin* is below, with *Jue Yin* wood in the spring source. *Bing-yin* and *bing-shen* enact the primary transformation in *yin*, and the oppositional transformation in *shen*. Its phase is frigid severity, and the water phase enacts the mandate of frigid severity. Its transformations are congealing desolation and biting cold—water in excess enacts these transformations. *Congealing* refers to ice and frost; *desolation*, to deep yin; *biting cold*, to extreme cold. Here, the water phase overcomes heavenly fire.

Its deviations are ice, snow, frost, and hail—deviations that exceed normal *qi*. Its virtues manifest as freezing and spreading transformations, while its killing force brings frost, snow, and hail prematurely, not awaiting winter. Its afflictions are cold-induced edema, rooted in the kidneys, and prolonged harm extends to the heart.

*Tai Yu* concludes with *bing-yin* and *bing-shen*. *Bing* governs the water phase, and *Yu* is the water tone. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years, hence *Tai Yu*. This is the *yuan* origin.

*Tai Jue* begins with *bing-yin* generating *ding-mao*, and *bing-shen* generating *ding-you*. *Ding* governs the wood phase, and *Jue* is the wood tone. *Mao* and *you* are yin years of insufficiency, which should be *Shao Jue*—yet they manifest as *Tai Jue*. This is because *mao* is the yearly convergence of wood, hence *mao* is *Tai* while *you* is *Shao*. This is the second *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Zhi* follows with *ding-mao* generating *wu-chen*, and *ding-you* generating *wu-xu*. *Wu* governs the fire phase, and *Zhi* is the fire tone. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Zhi*. This is the third *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Gong* follows with *wu-chen* generating *ji-si*, and *wu-xu* generating *ji-hai*. *Ji* governs the earth phase, and *Gong* is the earth tone. *Si* and *hai* are yin years of insufficiency, which should be *Shao Gong*—yet they manifest as *Tai Gong*. This is because *si* is the earthly gate of *si*. This is the fourth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Shang* follows with *ji-si* generating *geng-wu*, and *ji-hai* generating *geng-zi*. *Geng* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone. *Zi* and *wu* are yang years of excess, yet they manifest as *Shao Shang*—why? Because *wu* is fire, and *Shao Yin* presides over heaven, where fire imposes heavenly punishment, hence *Shao Shang*. This is the fifth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Yu* concludes with *geng-wu* generating *xin-wei*, and *geng-zi* generating *xin-chou*. *Xin* governs the water phase, and *Yu* is the water tone. *Xin* meets *bing* to harmonize the water phase and *Yu* tone. This completes the sixfold cycle, returning once more to *Yu*.

The Emperor said: Excellent. What of the governance of *Tai Yin*?
Qibo replied: It pertains to the *chou* and *wei* epochs. *Tai Yin* presides over heaven, and the wood phase governs *Tai Yin*, hence the first position.

*Shao Jue* is centered in the wood phase. *Tai Yang* is below, with *Tai Yang* in the spring source. The mutual overcoming of coolness and heat aligns with wood’s insufficiency—disaster befalls the three palaces. Metal enacts the mandate of clarity to overcome it, and the overcoming reaches its extreme. Fire arrives to counter-overcome, and wood is thereby harmonized. Thus, it is named *cool overcoming* and *heat counter-overcoming*.

In years of *Zheng Gong* insufficiency, earth governs heaven, and earth is balanced, hence *Zheng Gong*—all five positions align. *Ding-chou* and *ding-wei* enact the primary transformation in *wei*, and the oppositional transformation in *chou*. Its phase is wind, freezing, and heat—wind is the fundamental transformation of the wood phase. Freezing arises when Metal arrives to enact its overcoming transformation. Heat arises when fire counter-overcomes Metal, hence the three transformations.

*Zheng Jue* begins with *ding-chou* and *ding-wei*. *Ding* governs the wood phase, and *Jue* is the wood tone. *Chou* and *wei* are yin years, which should be insufficient, hence *Shao Jue*. Yet it is called *Zheng Jue* because *ding* originally resides in *wei*, named *stem-branch convergence*, and thus should be *Tai Jue*. As earth presides over heaven above, the wood phase submits to it, and half its *qi* returns to the earth phase—this is also called *Zheng Jue*. Thus, *wei* is *Zheng* while *chou* is *Shao*—these are the two explanations. This is the *yuan* origin.

*Tai Zhi* follows with *ding-chou* generating *wu-yin*, and *ding-wei* generating *wu-shen*. *Wu* governs the fire phase, and *Zhi* is the fire tone. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Zhi*. This is the second *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Gong* follows with *wu-yin* generating *ji-mao*, and *wu-shen* generating *ji-you*. *Ji* governs the earth phase, and *Gong* is the earth tone. *Mao* and *you* are yin years of insufficiency, hence *Shao Gong*. This is the third *yuan*.

*Tai Shang* follows with *ji-mao* generating *geng-chen*, and *ji-you* generating *geng-xu*. *Geng* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Shang*. This is the fourth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Yu* concludes with *geng-chen* generating *xin-si*, and *geng-xu* generating *xin-hai*. *Xin* governs the water phase, and *Yu* is the water tone.

*Si* and *hai* are yin years of insufficiency, hence *Shao Yu*. This is the fifth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Jue* begins with *xin-si* generating *ren-wu*, and *xin-hai* generating *ren-zi*. *Ren* governs the Wood phase, and *wu* being fire, Wood meets fire and becomes deficient, hence *Shao Jue*. *Ding* meets *ren*, combining into the Wood phase, completing the cycle and returning to *Jue*. *Tai Yin* governs the heavens, and with the fire phase under *Tai Yin*, this is the second sequence. *Shao Zheng* appears as the fire phase in the middle. *Tai Yang* below reveals *Tai Yang* water as the spring in the earth. Earth-water prevails over the fire phase. Cold and rain alternate in dominance, corresponding to fire’s insufficiency. Disaster strikes the ninth palace: when water’s cold mandate arrives to overcome, the dominance grows extreme, and earth’s rain transformation counteracts it, hence the term "cold and rain alternate in dominance." *Gui-chou* and *gui-wei* govern the proper transformation, with *chou* opposing transformation. Its phases are heat, cold, and rain: heat is the fire phase’s fundamental transformation; cold arises when water’s mandate overcomes fire; rain arises when earth’s mandate counteracts water. Thus, these three transformations operate. *Shao Zheng* in *gui-chou* and *gui-wei*: *gui* governs the fire phase, and *Zheng* is the fire tone. *Chou* and *wei* are yin years, hence *Shao Zheng*. Though *gui* in *chou* aligns with the direct sign, earth’s *Tai Yang* water overcomes it, hence *Shao Zheng*. This is the *yuan*’s inception.

*Tai Gong* follows with *gui-chou* generating *jia-yin*, and *gui-wei* generating *jia-shen*. *Jia* governs the earth phase, and *Gong* is the earth tone. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Gong*. This is the second *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Shang* follows with *jia-yin* generating *yi-mao*, and *jia-shen* generating *yi-you*. *Yi* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone. *Mao* and *you* are yin years, hence *Shao Shang*, but here it is *Tai Shang* because the heavens reveal *Yang Ming* Metal, combining with the celestial Metal as a *tian fu*, hence *Tai Shang*. This is the third *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Yu* concludes with *yi-mao* generating *bing-chen*, and *yi-you* generating *bing-xu*. *Bing* governs the water phase, and *Yu* is the water tone. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Yu*. This is the fourth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Jue* follows with *bing-chen* generating *ding-si*, and *bing-xu* generating *ding-hai*. *Ding* governs the Wood phase, and *Jue* is the Wood tone. *Si* and *hai* are yin years, hence *Shao Jue*, but here it is *Tai Jue* due to the celestial *tian fu*. This is the fifth *yuan*.

*Tai Zheng* follows with *ding-si* generating *wu-wu*, and *ding-hai* generating *wu-zi*. *Wu* meets *gui*, combining into the fire phase. This is the sixth *yuan*, returning to *Zheng*. *Tai Yin* governs the heavens, and with the earth phase under *Tai Yin*, this is the third sequence. *Shao Gong* appears as the earth phase in the middle. *Tai Yang* below reveals *Tai Yang* water as the spring in the earth, with earth ascending to unite with the heavens, countering the earth below. Wind and clarity alternate in dominance, corresponding to earth’s insufficiency. Disaster strikes the fifth palace: when Wood’s wind transformation arrives to overcome earth, the dominance grows extreme, and Metal’s clarity mandate counteracts Wood, restoring earth’s balance, hence the term "wind and clarity alternate in dominance." "Alternate" signifies Metal’s dominance, echoing the prior dominance. *Ji-chou* is a *Tai Yi Tian Fu*, as is *ji-wei*: *ji* governs the earth phase, *chou* and *wei* are earth years, and *Tai Yin* governs the heavens as earth, with all three converging, hence the name *Tai Yi Tian Fu*. Its phases are rain, wind, and frost: rain is earth’s fundamental mandate; wind arises when Wood overcomes earth; frost arises when Metal overcomes Wood. With the earth phase as a *tian fu*, only earth’s rain transforms independently, while wind and frost do not overcome. *Tai Gong* in *ji-chou* and *ji-wei*: *ji* governs the earth phase, and *Gong* is the earth tone. Aligning with the *tian fu*, hence *Tai Gong*. This is the *yuan*’s inception.

*Shao Shang* follows with *ji-chou* generating *geng-yin*, and *ji-wei* generating *geng-shen*. *Geng* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Shang*, but here it is *Shao Shang* because *yin* and *shen* reveal *Shao Yang* ministerial fire governing the heavens, termed *tian xing*, hence *Shao Shang*. This is the second *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Yu* concludes with *geng-yin* generating *xin-mao*, and *geng-shen* generating *xin-you*. *Xin* governs the water phase, and *Yu* is the water tone. *Mao* and *you* are yin years of insufficiency, hence *Shao Yu*. This is the third *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Jue* begins with *xin-mao* generating *ren-chen*, and *xin-you* generating *ren-xu*. *Ren* governs the Wood phase, and *Jue* is the Wood tone. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Jue*. This is the fourth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Zheng* follows with *ren-chen* generating *gui-si*, and *ren-xu* generating *gui-hai*. This is the second *yuan*.

*Tai Yin*, *Shao Shang*, *Tai Yang*, governing cold’s dominance and counteraction. *Yi-chou*, *yi-wei*: its phases are frost, heat, and cold.

*Tai Shang*, concluding *Tai Yu*, *Tai Jue*, *Shao Zheng*, *Tai Gong*, *Tai Shang*, *Tai Yin*, *Shao Yu*, *Tai Yang*, governing rain and wind’s alternation in dominance. *Xin-chou* and *xin-wei* govern the proper transformation, with *chou* opposing transformation. Its phases are cold, rain, and wind: cold is the water phase’s fundamental transformation; rain arises when earth overcomes water; wind arises when water counteracts earth. Thus, these three transformations operate. *Tai Yu* concludes in *xin-chou* and *xin-wei*: *xin* governs the water phase, and *Yu* is the water tone. *Chou* and *wei* are yin years, hence *Shao Yu*, but here it is *Tai Yu* because *Tai Yang* resides in the spring, uniting with the earth, hence *Tai Yu*. This is the *yuan*’s inception.

*Shao Jue* begins with *xin-chou* generating *ren-yin*, and *xin-wei* generating *ren-shen*. *Ren* governs the Wood phase, and *Jue* is the Wood tone. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years, but here it is *Shao Jue* because Wood meets fire and becomes deficient, aligning with the celestial fire, hence *Shao Jue*. This is the first *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Zheng* follows with *ren-yin* generating *gui-mao*, and *ren-shen* generating *gui-you*. *Gui* governs the fire phase, and *Zheng* is the fire tone. *Mao* and *you* are yin years, hence *Shao Zheng*, but here it is *Tai Zheng* because *mao* Wood generates fire, and fire prevails. This is the third *yuan*.

*Tai Gong* follows with *gui-mao* generating *jia-chen*, and *gui-you* generating *jia-xu*.

Here the *jia* governs the Earth phase, and *Gong* is the Earth tone. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Gong*. This is the fourth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Shang* follows with *jia-chen* generating *yi-si*, and *jia-xu* generating *yi-hai*. *Yi* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone. *Si* and *hai* are yin years of deficiency, hence *Shao Shang*. This is the fifth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Yu* concludes with *yi-si* generating *bing-wu*, and *yi-hai* generating *bing-zi*. *Bing* marks the end, *xin* the inception, and *bing* the completion of the Water phase. These six *yuan* complete the cycle of *Yu*’s return.

The Emperor said: "Excellent. What of the *Shao Yin*’s governance?"

Qi Bo replied: "This is the *zi-wu* cycle. *Shao Yin* presides over Heaven, and the Wood phase governs *Shao Yin*, hence it is the first. *Tai Jue* appears with the Wood phase at its center. *Yang Ming* is seen below as *Yang Ming* at the Spring. *Ren-zi* and *ren-wu* align with the *wu*’s central transformation, while *zi* corresponds to its opposition. Its *qi* stirs the wind, and the Wood phase enacts the wind’s transformative mandate. Its transformation is the rustling of silken banners, the splitting of buds—Wood receiving the first *qi* and giving rise to the myriad things. Thus, the wind rustles, silken banners flutter, buds split, and sprouts grow. Its aberration is violent uprooting and tearing—excess brings transformation. Wind injures Wood. Its afflictions manifest as distension and fullness; excess harms the liver, and over time, the spleen.

*Tai Jue* begins with *ren-zi* and *ren-wu*. *Ren* governs the Grain phase, and *Jue* is the Wood tone. *Zi* and *wu* are yang years, hence *Tai Jue* marks the inception of the *yuan*.

*Tai Zheng* follows with *ren-wu* generating *gui-wei*, and *ren-zi* generating *gui-chou*. *Gui* governs the Fire phase, and *Zheng* is the Fire tone. *Chou* and *wei* are yin years of deficiency, and should be *Shao Zheng*, but here it is *Tai Zheng* because *gui* in *chou* aligns with the stem-branch conjunction and the direct correspondence of the celestial tally. Thus, *chou* is *Tai* and *wei* is *Shao*, giving rise to two interpretations. This is the second *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Gong* follows with *gui-wei* generating *jia-shen*, and *gui-chou* generating *jia-yin*. *Jia* governs the Earth phase, and *Gong* is the Earth tone. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Gong*. This is the third *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Shang* follows with *jia-shen* generating *yi-you*, and *jia-yin* generating *yi-mao*. *Yi* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone. *Mao* and *you* are yin years of deficiency, and should be *Shao Shang*, but here it is *Tai Shang* because *Yang Ming* Metal presides over Heaven, enacting the celestial tally. This is the fourth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Yu* concludes with *yi-mao* generating *bing-chen*, and *yi-you* generating *bing-xu*. *Bing* governs the Water phase, and *Yu* is the Water tone. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Yu*. This is the fifth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Jue* follows with *bing-chen* generating *ding-si*, and *bing-xu* generating *ding-hai*. *Ding* governs the Wood phase, and *Jue* is the Wood tone. *Si* and *hai* are yin years of deficiency, and should be *Shao Jue*, but here it is *Tai Jue* because *Jue Yin* Wood presides over Heaven, and the phase aligns with the celestial tally. This *ding* meets *ren* to complete the cycle. *Shao Yin* presides over Heaven, and the Fire phase governs *Shao Yin*, hence it is the second. *Tai Zheng* appears with the Fire phase at its center. *Yang Ming* is seen below as *Yang Ming* at the Spring. *Wu-zi* is the celestial tally, and *wu-wu* is the grand celestial tally. The tally signifies conjunction. When the phase aligns with Heaven, it is called the celestial tally. When the year converges with the threefold conjunction, it is the grand celestial tally. Its *qi* blazes with scorching heat—excess and surplus align with Heaven, hence the fire *qi* flourishes in transformation, giving rise to scorching heat. Its transformation is radiant brilliance and oppressive heat—the Fire phase in excess manifests as blazing warmth and luminous clarity. Oppressive heat penetrates humanity, afflicting the people. Its aberration is searing conflagration and boiling tumult—transformation deviates from the norm. Scorching heat dominates transformation, and water boils like a seething cauldron. Its afflictions manifest as upper-body heat and blood overflow; excess harms the heart, and over time, the lungs.

*Tai Zheng* begins with *wu-zi* and *wu-wu*. *Wu* governs the Fire phase, and *Zheng* is the Fire tone. Thus, it marks the inception of the first *qi* of the *yuan*.

*Tai Gong* follows with *wu-wu* generating *ji-wei*, and *wu-zi* generating *ji-chou*. *Ji* governs the Earth phase. *Wei* and *chou* are yin years of deficiency, and should be *Shao Gong*, but here it is *Tai Gong* because *ji* in *wei* aligns with the stem-branch conjunction and the direct correspondence of the celestial tally. This is the second *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Shang* follows with *ji-wei* generating *geng-shen*, and *ji-chou* generating *geng-yin*. *Geng* governs the Metal phase, and *Shang* is the Metal tone. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years, and should be *Tai Shang*, but here it is *Shao Shang* because *Geng-shen* aligns with *Shao Yang* Minister Fire presiding over Heaven, enacting the celestial punishment, hence *Shao Shang*. This is the third *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Shao Yu* concludes with *geng-yin* generating *xin-mao*, and *geng-shen* generating *xin-you*. *Xin* governs the Water phase, and *Yu* is the Water tone. *Mao* and *you* are yin years of deficiency, hence *Shao Yu*. This is the fourth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Jue* begins with *xin-mao* generating *ren-chen*, and *xin-you* generating *ren-xu*. *Ren* governs the Wood phase, and *Jue* is the Wood tone. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years of excess, hence *Tai Jue*. This is the fifth *yuan* of generative assistance.

*Tai Zheng* follows with *ren-chen* generating *gui-si*, and *ren-xu* generating *gui-hai*. *Gui* governs the Fire phase, and *Zheng* is the Fire tone. *Si* and *hai* are yin years of deficiency, and should be *Shao Zheng*, but here it is *Tai Zheng* because *si* aligns with Fire, and the branch harmonizes with the stem’s virtue. Thus, *gui* meets *wu*, and *wu-gui* governs the Fire phase. This is the sixth *yuan*. *Zheng* completes the cycle.

*Shao Yin* presides over Heaven, and the Earth phase governs *Shao Yin*, hence it is the third. *Tai Gong* appears with the Earth phase at its center. *Yang Ming* is seen below as *Yang Ming* at the Spring. *Jia-zi* and *jia-wu* align with the *wu*’s central transformation, while *zi* corresponds to its opposition. Its *qi* brings overcast rain, and the Earth phase enacts the dampness’s transformative mandate, hence overcast rain. Its transformation is gentle moisture and timely rain—the Earth phase softens the heat, and dust settles into dampness. Thus, it is gentle and moist. By the fourth *qi*, great rains fall in season. Its aberration is violent storms and thunderous shocks—transformation deviates from the norm. Excess and surplus bring sudden downpours, thunder, and hail, as Earth prevails in its victory. Its afflictions manifest as abdominal fullness and bodily heaviness; excess harms the spleen, and over time, the kidneys.

**Tai Gong in Jia-zi and Jia-wu years.**
*Jia* governs the Earth phase, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth. *Zi* and *wu* are yang years, hence *Tai Gong* (Great Palace). This is the Primordial Origin.

**Shao Shang in this Jia-zi begets Yi-chou, Jia-wu begets Yi-wei.**
*Yi* governs the Metal phase, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal. *Chou* and *wei* are yin years, deficient, hence *Shao Shang* (Lesser Note). This is the Second Origin of Generation.

**Tai Yu concludes this: Yi-chou begets Bing-yin, Yi-wei begets Bing-shen.**
*Bing* governs the Water phase, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years, excessive, hence *Tai Yu* (Great Flourish). This is the Third Origin of Generation.

**Tai Jiao begins this: Bing-yin begets Ding-mao, Bing-shen begets Ding-you.**
*Ding* governs the Wood phase, corresponding to the *Jiao* tone of Wood. *Mao* and *you* are yin years, which should be *Shao Jiao* (Lesser Angle), but here it is *Tai Jiao*—for *mao* belongs to Wood, aligning with the phase in a Yearly Convergence, hence *Tai Jiao*. This is the Fourth Origin of Generation.

**Tai Zhi in this: Ding-mao begets Wu-chen, Ding-you begets Wu-xu.**
*Wu* governs the Fire phase, corresponding to the *Zhi* tone of Fire. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years, hence *Tai Zhi* (Great Governance). This is the Fifth Origin of Generation.

**Tai Gong in this: Wu-chen begets Ji-si, Wu-xu begets Ji-hai.**
*Ji* governs the Earth phase, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth. *Si* and *hai* are yin years, which should be *Shao Gong* (Lesser Palace), but here it is *Tai Gong*—for the sixth *si* is the Earthly Portal, and *Ji* matches *si*, hence *Tai Gong*. *Ji* meets *Jia* to harmonize the Earth phase. This is the Sixth Origin, completing the cycle.

**The Palace returns to its full circuit.**
*Shao Yin* governs Heaven, Metal phase under *Shao Yin*, hence the fourth position. *Tai Shang* (Great Note) appears at the center as the Metal phase. *Yang Ming* is seen below as *Yang Ming* at the Spring. *Geng-zi* and *geng-wu* align with the *wu*’s central transformation, while *zi* corresponds to its opposition. Its *qi* brings freezing vigor, as the Metal phase enacts the clear and bracing transformation. Its manifestation is mist and dew, desolate and stirring—the Metal phase in motion; white haze like mist, Metal winds sighing audibly. Its aberration is stern desolation and withering: when Metal’s wrath arises, transformation deviates into desolation and decay, for Metal’s *qi* prevails, and verdant growth withers. Its afflictions manifest as upper-clearance disorders affecting the lungs, and over time, the liver.

**Shao Shang in Geng-zi and Geng-wu years.**
*Geng* governs the Metal phase, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal. *Zi* and *wu* are yang years, which should be *Tai Shang* (Great Note), but here it is *Shao Shang*—for *Shao Yin* Sovereign Fire governs Heaven, imposing celestial punishment, hence *Shao Shang*. This is the Primordial Origin.

**Shao Yu concludes this: Geng-zi begets Xin-chou, Geng-wu begets Xin-wei.**
*Xin* governs the Water phase, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. *Chou* and *wei* are yin years, deficient, hence *Shao Yu* (Lesser Flourish). This is the Second Origin of Generation.

**Shao Jiao begins this: Xin-chou begets Ren-yin, Xin-wei begets Ren-shen.**
*Ren* governs the Wood phase, corresponding to the *Jiao* tone of Wood. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years, which should be *Tai Jiao* (Great Angle), but here it is *Shao Jiao*—why? *Shao Yang* Ministerial Fire governs Heaven, and Fire scorches Wood, hence *Shao Jiao*. This is the Third Origin of Generation.

**Tai Zhi in this: Ren-yin begets Gui-mao, Ren-shen begets Gui-you.**
*Gui* governs the Fire phase, corresponding to the *Zhi* tone of Fire. *Mao* and *you* are yin years, which should be *Shao Zhi* (Lesser Governance), but here it is *Tai Zhi*—why? *Mao* Wood engenders Fire, hence *Tai Zhi*. This is the Fourth Origin of Generation.

**Tai Gong in this: Gui-mao begets Jia-chen, Gui-you begets Jia-xu.**
*Jia* governs the Earth phase, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years, excessive, hence *Tai Gong*. This is the Fifth Origin of Generation.

**Shao Shang in this: Jia-chen begets Yi-si, Jia-xu begets Yi-hai.**
*Yi* governs the Metal phase, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal. *Yi* and *geng* harmonize the Metal phase. This is the Sixth Origin, completing the cycle.

**Shao Yin governs Heaven, Water phase under Shao Yin, hence the fifth position.**
*Tai Yu* (Great Flourish) appears at the center as the Water phase. *Yang Ming* is seen below as *Yang Ming* at the Spring. In the *Bing-zi* Yearly Convergence, Water phase aligns with the Heavenly Stem, a convergence of phase and year, hence the Yearly Convergence. *Bing-wu* aligns with central transformation. Its *qi* brings cold, as the Water phase enacts the frigid transformation. Its manifestation is congealing desolation and biting cold—Water in excess, ice solidifies, the heavens grow bleak and bitter, the cold reaches its extreme. Its aberration is ice, snow, frost, and hail: when transformation loses its norm, the cold’s virtue prevails, manifesting as frost and snow, while Water’s hail brings destructive transformation. Its afflictions manifest as cold and lower-cold dampness affecting the kidneys, and over time, the heart.

**Tai Yu concludes in Bing-zi and Bing-wu years.**
*Bing* governs the Water phase, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. *Zi* and *wu* are yang years, hence *Tai Yu*. This is the Primordial Origin.

**Tai Jiao begins this: Bing-zi begets Ding-chou, Bing-wu begets Ding-wei.**
*Ding* governs the Wood phase, corresponding to the *Jiao* tone of Wood. *Chou* and *wei* are yin years, which should be *Shao Jiao* (Lesser Angle), but here *Ding* is lodged in *wei*, hence *Tai Jiao*. This is the Second Origin of Generation.

**Tai Zhi in this: Ding-chou begets Wu-yin, Ding-wei begets Wu-shen.**
*Wu* governs the Fire phase, corresponding to the *Zhi* tone of Fire. *Yin* and *shen* are yang years, excessive, hence *Tai Zhi*. This is the Third Origin of Generation.

**Shao Gong in this: Wu-yin begets Ji-mao, Wu-shen begets Ji-you.**
*Ji* governs the Earth phase, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth. *Mao* and *you* are yin years, deficient, hence *Shao Gong*. This is the Fourth Origin of Generation.

**Tai Shang in this: Ji-mao begets Geng-chen, Ji-you begets Geng-xu.**
*Geng* governs the Metal phase, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal. *Chen* and *xu* are yang years, excessive, hence *Tai Shang*. This is the Fifth Origin of Generation.

**Shao Yu in this: Geng-chen begets Xin-si, Geng-xu begets Xin-hai.**
*Xin* governs the Water phase, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. *Xin* phase aligns with *bing*, and *bing* and *xin* share the *Yu* tone. This is the Sixth Origin, completing the cycle.

The Emperor said: "Excellent. What of the governance of *Jue Yin*?"
Qi Bo replied: "The *si-hai* cycle. *Jue Yin* governs Heaven, Wood phase under *Jue Yin*, hence the first position. *Shao Jiao* (Lesser Angle) appears at the center as the Wood phase. *Shao Yang* is seen below as *Shao Yang* at the Spring. The interplay of cool and heat, victory and restoration, aligns with Wood’s deficiency: disasters strike the three palaces. That is, Metal’s clear transformation comes to vanquish Wood, and the victory is extreme. Wood has its child—Fire’s hot transformation restores victory over Metal, and Wood is thus harmonized. Hence it is said: cool and heat, victory and restoration, align."

In years where *Jue Yin* governs Heaven and Wood is deficient, Wood above attains balance. *Ding-si* is a *tianfu* year of dual transformation; *Ding-hai* is a *tianfu* year of proper transformation. Their *qi* movements manifest as wind, cold, heat, and wind—these are the fundamental transformations of Wood. Cold arises when Metal’s command overcomes Wood; heat arises when Fire’s command restores victory over Metal. Thus these two transformations occur.

*Tai Jiao* begins with *Ding-si* and *Ding-hai*. *Ding* governs Wood’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Jiao* tone of Wood. Though *si* and *hai* are Yin years of deficiency, they should be *Shao Jiao*, yet here they are *Tai Jiao*—this is because *Jue Yin* Wood aligns with the *tianfu*, hence *Tai Jiao*. This is the First Origin.

*Tai Zhi* follows: *Ding-si* generates *Wu-wu*, and *Ding-hai* generates *Wu-zi*. *Wu* governs Fire’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Zhi* tone of Fire. *Zi* and *wu* are Yang years of excess, hence *Tai Zhi*. This is the Second Origin of mutual generation.

*Tai Gong* follows: *Wu-wu* generates *Ji-wei*, and *Wu-zi* generates *Ji-chou*. *Ji* governs Earth’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth. Though *chou* and *wei* are Yin years of deficiency, here they are *Tai Gong*—this is because *Ji* lodges in *wei*, and the stems mutually generate, making *wei* *Tai* and *chou* *Shao*. This is the Second Origin of mutual generation.

*Shao Shang* follows: *Ji-chou* generates *Geng-yin*, and *Ji-wei* generates *Geng-shen*. *Geng* governs Metal’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal. Though *yin* and *shen* are Yang years and should be *Tai Shang*, here they are *Shao Shang*—this is because *Shao Yang* Ministerial Fire governs Heaven above, imposing celestial punishment, hence *Shao Shang*. This is the Fourth Origin of mutual generation.

*Shao Yu* concludes: *Geng-yin* generates *Xin-mao*, and *Geng-shen* generates *Xin-you*. *Xin* governs Water’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. *Mao* and *you* are Yin years of deficiency, hence *Shao Yu*. This is the Fifth Origin of mutual generation.

*Tai Jiao* begins anew: *Xin-mao* generates *Ren-chen*, and *Xin-you* generates *Ren-xu*. *Ren* governs Wood’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Jiao* tone of Wood. Here *Ding* reappears, and *Ren* aligns with Wood’s *qi*. This is the Sixth Origin, completing the cycle and returning to the beginning.

When *Jue Yin* governs Heaven and Fire’s *qi* aligns with *Jue Yin*, it occupies the second position. *Shao Zhi* appears at the center as Fire’s *qi*. *Shao Yang* is seen below as *Shao Yang* at the Spring. The interplay of cold and rain, victory and restoration, aligns with Fire’s deficiency: disasters strike the nine palaces. That is, Water’s cold command comes to vanquish Fire, and the victory is extreme. Earth’s rain command restores victory over Water, and Fire is thus harmonized. Hence it is said: cold and rain, victory and restoration, align.

*Gui-si* is a year of dual transformation; *Gui-hai* is without transformation. Their *qi* movements manifest as heat, cold, and rain—these are the fundamental transformations of Fire. Cold arises when Water’s command overcomes Fire; rain arises when Earth’s command restores victory over Water. Thus these three transformations occur.

*Tai Zhi* in *Gui-si* and *Gui-hai*. *Gui* governs Fire’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Zhi* tone of Fire. Though *si* and *hai* are Yin years of deficiency and should be *Shao Zhi*, here they are *Tai Zhi*—this is because *Shao Yang* Ministerial Fire governs below at the Spring, aligning with Fire’s *qi* in a *suihui* year, hence *Tai Zhi*.

*Tai Gong* follows: *Gui-si* generates *Jia-wu*, and *Gui-hai* generates *Jia-zi*. *Jia* governs Earth’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth. *Zi* and *wu* are Yang years of excess, hence *Tai Gong*. This is the Second Origin of mutual generation.

*Shao Shang* follows: *Jia-wu* generates *Yi-wei*, and *Jia-zi* generates *Yi-chou*. *Yi* governs Metal’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal. *Chou* and *wei* are Yin years of deficiency, hence *Shao Shang*. This is the Third Origin of mutual generation.

*Tai Yu* concludes: *Yi-chou* generates *Bing-yin*, and *Yi-wei* generates *Bing-shen*. *Bing* governs Water’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. *Yin* and *shen* are Yang years of excess, hence *Tai Yu*. This is the Fourth Origin of mutual generation.

*Tai Jiao* begins: *Bing-yin* generates *Ding-mao*, and *Bing-shen* generates *Ding-you*. *Ding* governs Wood’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Jiao* tone of Wood. Though *mao* and *you* are Yin years and should be *Shao Jiao*, here they are *Tai Jiao*—this is because *mao* aligns with Wood’s *qi* in a *suihui* year, hence *Tai Jiao*. This is the Fifth Origin of mutual generation.

*Tai Zhi* follows: *Ding-mao* generates *Wu-chen*, and *Ding-you* generates *Wu-xu*. *Wu* governs Fire’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Zhi* tone of Fire. Here *Gui* begins and *Wu* concludes, with *Wu* and *Gui* aligning in Fire’s *qi*. This is the Sixth Origin, completing the cycle.

When *Jue Yin* governs Heaven and Earth’s *qi* aligns with *Jue Yin*, it occupies the third position. *Shao Gong* appears at the center as Earth’s *qi*. *Shao Yang* is seen below as *Shao Yang* at the Spring. The interplay of wind and clear *qi*, victory and restoration, aligns with Earth’s deficiency: disasters strike the five palaces. That is, Wood’s wind command comes to vanquish Earth, and the victory is extreme. Metal’s clear command restores victory over Wood, and Earth is thus harmonized. Hence it is said: wind and clear *qi*, victory and restoration, align.

*Ji-si* and *Ji-hai* are years of dual transformation; *hai* is a year of proper transformation. Their *qi* movements manifest as rain, wind, and cold—these are the fundamental transformations of Earth. Wind arises when Wood overcomes Earth; cold arises when Metal restores victory over Wood. Thus these two transformations—rain, wind, and cold—occur.

*Tai Gong* in *Ji-si* and *Ji-hai*. *Ji* governs Earth’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth.

In *Si-Hai* yin years, the phase should be *Lesser Gong*, yet here it is *Greater Gong*—this is because the sixth *Si* resides in Earth’s gate, hence *Greater Gong*. This is the *Primordial Origin*.

*Lesser Shang* begins with *Ji-Si* giving rise to *Geng-Wu*, and *Ji-Hai* giving rise to *Geng-Zi*. *Geng* governs Metal’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal.

In *Zi-Wu* yang years, the phase should be *Greater Shang*, yet here it is *Lesser Shang*—this is because *Lesser Yin* Sovereign Fire governs the heavens above, imposing celestial punishment, hence *Lesser Shang*. This is the *First Nourishing Cycle* of *Resource and Generation*.

*Lesser Yu* concludes with *Geng-Wu* giving rise to *Xin-Wei*, and *Geng-Zi* giving rise to *Xin-Chou*. *Xin* governs Water’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. *Chou-Wei* are yin years of deficiency, hence *Lesser Yu*. This is the *Third Nourishing Cycle* of *Resource and Generation*.

*Lesser Jue* begins with *Xin-Chou* giving rise to *Ren-Yin*, and *Xin-Wei* giving rise to *Ren-Shen*. *Ren* governs Wood’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Jue* tone of Wood. In *Yin-Shen* yang years, the phase should be *Greater Jue*, yet here it is *Lesser Jue*—this is because *Lesser Yang* Ministerial Fire governs the heavens above in *Yin-Shen*, and fire’s excess scorches Wood, hence *Lesser Jue*. This is the *Fifth Nourishing Cycle* of *Resource and Generation*.

*Greater Zhi* begins with *Ren-Yin* giving rise to *Gui-Mao*, and *Ren-Shen* giving rise to *Gui-You*. *Gui* governs Fire’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Zhi* tone of Fire. In *Mao-You* yin years, the phase should be *Lesser Zhi*, yet here it is *Greater Zhi*—this is because *Mao* belongs to Wood, and Fire encounters Wood in its flourishing phase, hence *Greater Zhi*, which is the yearly generation. This is the *Fifth Cycle* of *Resource and Generation*.

*Greater Gong* begins with *Gui-Mao* giving rise to *Jia-Chen*, and *Gui-You* giving rise to *Jia-Xu*. *Jia* governs Earth’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth. In *Chen-Xu* yang years, the phase should be *Greater Gong*. Here, *Jia* returns to *Ji*, completing the cycle of Earth’s *Gong* phase.

*Jueyin* governs the heavens above, and Metal’s *qi* governs *Jueyin*, hence the fourth phase. *Lesser Shang* is centered in Metal’s *qi*. *Lesser Yang* is seen below as *Lesser Yang* at the spring, where Earth’s fire subdues Metal’s *qi*.

Heat and cold, victory and restoration, align with Metal’s deficiency: disasters strike the seven palaces. That is, Fire’s heat command comes to vanquish Metal, and the victory is extreme. Water’s cold command restores victory over Fire, and Metal is thus harmonized. Hence it is said: heat and cold, victory and restoration, align.

*Yi-Si* and *Yi-Hai* are years of dual transformation; *Hai* is a year of proper transformation. Their *qi* movements manifest as cold, heat, and cold—these are the fundamental transformations of Metal. Heat arises when Fire overcomes Metal; cold arises when Water restores victory over Fire. Thus these two transformations—cold, heat, and cold—occur.

*Lesser Shang* in *Yi-Si* and *Yi-Hai*. *Yi* governs Metal’s *qi*, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal.

The *Yi-Si* and *Yi-Hai* years are years of Metal’s deficiency, hence *Lesser Shang*. They mark the inception. The *Tai-Yu* concludes with *Yi-Si* generating *Bing-Wu* and *Yi-Hai* generating *Bing-Zi*. *Bing* governs the Water *qi*, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. The *Zi* and *Wu* years are yang, hence *Tai-Yu*. This is the second cycle of generative assistance.

The *Tai-Jiao* begins with *Bing-Wu* generating *Ding-Wei* and *Bing-Zi* generating *Ding-Chou*. *Ding* governs the Wood *qi*, corresponding to the *Jiao* tone of Wood. The *Chou* and *Wei* years are yin; they should be *Lesser Jiao*, but here they are *Tai-Jiao* because *Ding* is lodged in *Wei*, aligning with the heavenly stems and thus forming a direct resonance. This is the third cycle of generative assistance.

The *Tai-Zhi* follows with *Ding-Wei* generating *Wu-Shen* and *Ding-Chou* generating *Wu-Yin*. *Wu* governs the Fire *qi*, corresponding to the *Zhi* tone of Fire. The *Yin* and *Shen* years are yang and excessive, hence *Tai-Zhi*. This is the fourth cycle.

The *Lesser Gong* arises from *Wu-Yin* generating *Ji-Mao* and *Wu-Shen* generating *Ji-You*. *Ji* governs the Earth *qi*, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth. The *Mao* and *You* years are yin and deficient, hence *Lesser Gong*. This is the third cycle of generative assistance.

The *Tai-Shang* follows with *Ji-Mao* generating *Geng-Chen* and *Ji-You* generating *Geng-Xu*. *Geng* governs the Metal *qi*, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal. The cycle begins with *Yi* and concludes with *Geng*; *Yi* and *Geng* unite in Metal, completing the *Shang* cycle. As *Jueyin* governs the heavens and Water *qi* aligns with *Jueyin*, this is the fifth cycle. *Lesser Yu* manifests with Water *qi* at its center.

With *Shaoyang* governing below as the *qi* in the springs, Water overcomes the Earth Fire. Rain and wind, victory and restoration, align with Water’s deficiency: disasters strike the first palace. That is, Earth’s rain command comes to vanquish Water, and the victory is extreme. Water, thus besieged, is restored by Wood’s wind command, and Water is harmonized. Hence it is said: rain and wind, victory and restoration, align.

The *Xin-Si* and *Xin-Hai* years are years of dual transformation; *Hai* is a year of proper transformation. Their *qi* movements manifest as cold, rain, and wind—these are the transformations of Water. Rain arises when Earth overcomes Water; wind arises when Wood restores victory over Earth. Thus these three transformations occur.

The *Lesser Yu* concludes with *Xin-Si* and *Xin-Hai*. *Xin* governs the Water *qi*, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. The *Si* and *Hai* years are yin, hence *Lesser Yu*. This marks the inception.

The *Lesser Jiao* begins with *Xin-Si* generating *Ren-Wu* and *Xin-Hai* generating *Ren-Zi*. *Ren* governs the Wood *qi*, corresponding to the *Jiao* tone of Wood. The *Zi* and *Wu* years are yang and should be *Tai-Jiao*, but here they are *Lesser Jiao* because *Shaoyin* Fire governs above, and Fire restrains Wood, diminishing it. This is the second cycle of generative assistance.

The *Tai-Zhi* follows with *Ren-Wu* generating *Gui-Wei* and *Ren-Zi* generating *Gui-Chou*. *Gui* governs the Fire *qi*, corresponding to the *Zhi* tone of Fire. The *Chou* and *Wei* years are yin and should be deficient, but here they are *Tai-Zhi* because *Gui* is lodged in *Chou*, aligning with the heavenly stems and thus forming a direct resonance. This is the third cycle.

The *Lesser Gong* arises from *Gui-Chou* generating *Jia-Yin* and *Gui-Wei* generating *Jia-Shen*. *Jia* governs the Earth *qi*, corresponding to the *Gong* tone of Earth. The *Yin* and *Shen* years are yang and excessive, and should be *Tai-Gong*. Here they are *Lesser Gong* because *Jia* encounters *Shen*’s punishment, thus diminishing it. This is a year of restraint. This is the fourth cycle of generative assistance.

The *Tai-Shang* follows with *Jia-Shen* generating *Yi-You* and *Jia-Yin* generating *Yi-Mao*. *Yi* governs the Metal *qi*, corresponding to the *Shang* tone of Metal. The *Mao* and *You* years are yin and deficient, and should be *Lesser Shang*, but here they are *Tai-Shang* because *Yangming* Metal governs the heavens above, forming a heavenly resonance with the *qi* of the year. This is the fifth cycle.

The *Tai-Yu* concludes with *Yi-Mao* generating *Bing-Chen* and *Yi-You* generating *Bing-Xu*. *Bing* governs the Water *qi*, corresponding to the *Yu* tone of Water. The *Chen* and *Xu* years are yang, hence *Tai-Yu*. The cycle begins with *Xin* and concludes with *Bing*; *Bing* and *Xin* unite in Water, completing the *Yu* cycle.

*The Seventeenth Scroll of the Mysterious Pearl of the Six Qi in the Plain Questions Concludes.*
